```go
// GUID pool for high-performance event generation
type GuidPool struct {
	guids []GUID
	index int
	size  int
}

var globalGuidPool *GuidPool

// InitializeGuidPool creates a pool of pre-generated GUIDs for performance
func InitializeGuidPool(size int) {
	globalGuidPool = &GuidPool{
		guids: make([]GUID, size),
		index: 0,
		size:  size,
	}

	// Pre-generate all GUIDs
	for i := 0; i < size; i++ {
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&globalGuidPool.guids[i])))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to pre-generate GUID %d: %d", i, hr)
		}
	}
	log.Printf("Initialized GUID pool with %d GUIDs", size)
}

// GetNextGuid returns the next GUID from the pool (cycling)
func GetNextGuid() *GUID {
	if globalGuidPool == nil {
		InitializeGuidPool(10000) // Default pool size
	}

	guid := &globalGuidPool.guids[globalGuidPool.index]
	globalGuidPool.index = (globalGuidPool.index + 1) % globalGuidPool.size
	return guid
}

// Pre-computed UTF16 strings for common values
var (
	precomputedStrings = map[string][]uint16{
		"ImInYourLogsNow":     syscall.StringToUTF16("ImInYourLogsNow"),
		"PropertyBag":         syscall.StringToUTF16("PropertyBag"),
		"file":                syscall.StringToUTF16("file"),
		"0":                   syscall.StringToUTF16("0"),
		"|":                   syscall.StringToUTF16("|"),
		"SchemaParamFilePath": syscall.StringToUTF16("SchemaParamFilePath"),
	}
)

// GetPrecomputedUTF16 returns pre-converted UTF16 string or converts on demand
func GetPrecomputedUTF16(s string) []uint16 {
	if utf16, exists := precomputedStrings[s]; exists {
		return utf16
	}
	return syscall.StringToUTF16(s)
}

// GetProviderStatsTable returns the statistics table as a formatted string for TUI display
func GetProviderStatsTable() string {
	statsMutex.RLock()
	defer statsMutex.RUnlock()

	var result strings.Builder

	result.WriteString("â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”\n")

	totalSuccess := int64(0)
	totalFailures := int64(0)

	// Specific order for providers
	providerOrder := []string{
		"Antimalware-Threat",
		"Antimalware-Benign",
		"LDAP-Client",
		"TCP/IP-Network",
		"WMI-Activity",
		"AMSI-Events",
		"DPAPI-Crypto",

			stats.mutex.RLock()

			failures := stats.Failures
			total := success + failures
			rate := stats.Rate
			stats.mutex.RUnlock()

			totalSuccess += success
			totalFailures += failures

			result.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("â”‚ %-22s â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8.1f    â”‚\n",
				name, success, failures, total, rate))
		}
	}

	result.WriteString("â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¼â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤\n")
	result.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("â”‚ %-22s â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %8d â”‚ %-11s â”‚\n",
		"TOTAL", totalSuccess, totalFailures, totalSuccess+totalFailures, ""))
	result.WriteString("â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜\n")
	result.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("Last updated: %s", time.Now().Format("15:04:05")))

	return result.String()
}

// GetWindowsErrorDescription returns a descriptive name for Windows error codes
func GetWindowsErrorDescription(errorCode uint32) string {
	switch errorCode {
	case 0:
		return "ERROR_SUCCESS (0)"
	case 1:
		return "ERROR_INVALID_FUNCTION (1)"
	case 2:
		return "ERROR_FILE_NOT_FOUND (2)"
	case 3:
		return "ERROR_PATH_NOT_FOUND (3)"
	case 4:
		return "ERROR_TOO_MANY_OPEN_FILES (4)"
	case 5:
		return "ERROR_ACCESS_DENIED (5)"
	case 6:
		return "ERROR_INVALID_HANDLE (6)"
	case 7:
		return "ERROR_ARENA_TRASHED (7)"
	case 8:
		return "ERROR_NOT_ENOUGH_MEMORY (8)"
	case 9:
		return "ERROR_INVALID_BLOCK (9)"
	case 10:
		return "ERROR_BAD_ENVIRONMENT (10)"
	case 11:
		return "ERROR_BAD_FORMAT (11)"
	case 12:
		return "ERROR_INVALID_ACCESS (12)"
	case 13:
		return "ERROR_INVALID_DATA (13)"
	case 14:
		return "ERROR_OUTOFMEMORY (14)"
	case 50:
		return "ERROR_NOT_SUPPORTED (50)"
	case 87:
		return "ERROR_INVALID_PARAMETER (87)"
	case 122:
		return "ERROR_INSUFFICIENT_BUFFER (122)"
	case 183:
		return "ERROR_ALREADY_EXISTS (183)"
	case 234:
		return "ERROR_MORE_DATA (234)"
	case 534:
		return "ERROR_ARITHMETIC_OVERFLOW (534)"
	case 1450:
		return "ERROR_NO_SYSTEM_RESOURCES (1450)"
	case 1816:
		return "ERROR_NOT_ENOUGH_QUOTA (1816)"
	// ETW-specific error codes
	case 0x80070005:
		return "E_ACCESSDENIED (0x80070005)"
	case 0x80070008:
		return "E_OUTOFMEMORY (0x80070008)"
	case 0x80070057:
		return "E_INVALIDARG (0x80070057)"
	case 0x8007007A:
		return "ERROR_INSUFFICIENT_BUFFER (0x8007007A)"
	case 0x800700EA:
		return "ERROR_MORE_DATA (0x800700EA)"
	case 0xC0000005:
		return "STATUS_ACCESS_VIOLATION (0xC0000005)"
	case 0xC000009A:
		return "STATUS_INSUFFICIENT_RESOURCES (0xC000009A)"
	case 0xC0000017:
		return "STATUS_NO_MEMORY (0xC0000017)"
	case 0xC000016A:
		return "STATUS_LOG_FILE_FULL (0xC000016A)"
	default:
		return fmt.Sprintf("UNKNOWN_ERROR (%d)", errorCode)
	}
}

// IsRunningAsAdmin checks if the current process is running with administrator privileges
func IsRunningAsAdmin() bool {
	currentProcess, _, _ := procGetCurrentProcess.Call()
	if currentProcess == 0 {
		return false
	}

	var token syscall.Handle
	ret, _, _ := procOpenProcessToken.Call(
		currentProcess,
		TOKEN_QUERY,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&token)),
	)
	if ret == 0 {
		return false
	}
	defer syscall.CloseHandle(token)

	var elevationType uint32
	var returnedLen uint32
	ret, _, _ = procGetTokenInformation.Call(
		uintptr(token),
		TokenElevationType,
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&elevationType)),
		4, // sizeof(uint32)
		uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&returnedLen)),
	)
	if ret == 0 {
		return false
	}

	return elevationType == TokenElevationTypeFull
}
```

```go
// WriteRandomPowerShellEvent generates spam PowerShell events
func WriteRandomPowerShellEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting PowerShell Commandlet events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&PowerShellProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register PowerShell provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 50; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		// Randomly choose between event 7937 (Commandlet) and 16385 (AMSI)
		if rand.Intn(2) == 0 {
			// Event 7937 - Commandlet
			contextInfo := randomContextInfo()
			userData := randomUserData()
			payload := randomPowerShellPayload()

			LogPowerShellCommandletEvent(regHandle, contextInfo, userData, payload, i, true)
		} else {
			// Event 16385 - AMSI
			action := randomAmsiAction()
			amsiContext := randomAmsiContext()

			LogPowerShellAmsiEvent(regHandle, action, amsiContext, i, true)
		}
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

// WriteInfiniteRandomPowerShellEvent generates infinite PowerShell events for buffer overflow mode
func WriteInfiniteRandomPowerShellEvent() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&PowerShellProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register PowerShell provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		activityId := GetNextGuid()
		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(activityId)))

		// Randomly choose between event types
		var success bool
		var providerName string
		if rand.Intn(2) == 0 {
			// Event 7937 - Commandlet
			contextInfo := randomContextInfo()
			userData := randomUserData()
			payload := randomPowerShellPayload()

			success = LogPowerShellCommandletEventQuiet(regHandle, contextInfo, userData, payload, count)
			providerName = "PowerShell-Commandlet"
		} else {
			// Event 16385 - AMSI
			action := randomAmsiAction()
			amsiContext := randomAmsiContext()

			success = LogPowerShellAmsiEventQuiet(regHandle, action, amsiContext, count)
			providerName = "PowerShell-Amsi"
		}

		UpdateProviderStats(providerName, success)
		count++
	}
}

// WritePowerShellEvent generates a single PowerShell event
func WritePowerShellEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting PowerShell Commandlet events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&PowerShellProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register PowerShell provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	// Generate a single event 7937 (Commandlet)
	contextInfo := "Script Block ID: 12345678-1234-5678-9012-123456789012"
	userData := "User: DOMAIN\\admin"
	payload := "Invoke-Mimikatz -Command '\"sekurlsa::logonpasswords\"'"

	LogPowerShellCommandletEvent(regHandle, contextInfo, userData, payload, 0, true)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

// LogPowerShellCommandletEvent logs event ID 7937 (Commandlet)
func LogPowerShellCommandletEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, contextInfo, userData, payload string, iteration int, verbose bool) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 7937
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(contextInfo)))), Size: uint32((len(contextInfo) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(userData)))), Size: uint32((len(userData) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(payload)))), Size: uint32((len(payload) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	if verbose {
		log.Printf("ContextInfo: %s", contextInfo)
		log.Printf("UserData: %s", userData)
		log.Printf("Payload: %s", payload)
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write PowerShell Commandlet event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("PowerShell Commandlet Event %d written successfully.", iteration)
	}
}

// LogPowerShellCommandletEventQuiet is a quiet version for TUI mode
func LogPowerShellCommandletEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, contextInfo, userData, payload string, iteration int) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 7937
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(contextInfo)))), Size: uint32((len(contextInfo) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(userData)))), Size: uint32((len(userData) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(payload)))), Size: uint32((len(payload) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return status == 0
}

// LogPowerShellAmsiEvent logs event ID 16385 (AMSI)
func LogPowerShellAmsiEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, action, amsiContext string, iteration int, verbose bool) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 16385
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000000000000

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(action)))), Size: uint32((len(action) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(amsiContext)))), Size: uint32((len(amsiContext) + 1) * 2)},
	}

	if verbose {
		log.Printf("Action: %s", action)
		log.Printf("AmsiContext: %s", amsiContext)
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write PowerShell AMSI event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("PowerShell AMSI Event %d written successfully.", iteration)
	}
}
```

`cmd/rpc.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"encoding/hex"
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

var RPCProviderGuid = GUID{0x6ad52b32, 0xd609, 0x4be9, [8]byte{0xae, 0x07, 0xce, 0x8d, 0xae, 0x93, 0x7e, 0x39}}

func WriteRPCFunctionTraceEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting Microsoft-Windows-RPC function trace event...")

	// Log the provider GUID we're using
	log.Printf("Provider GUID: {%08x-%04x-%04x-%02x%02x-%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x}",
		RPCProviderGuid.Data1, RPCProviderGuid.Data2, RPCProviderGuid.Data3,
		RPCProviderGuid.Data4[0], RPCProviderGuid.Data4[1], RPCProviderGuid.Data4[2], RPCProviderGuid.Data4[3],
		RPCProviderGuid.Data4[4], RPCProviderGuid.Data4[5], RPCProviderGuid.Data4[6], RPCProviderGuid.Data4[7])

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&RPCProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register Microsoft-Windows-RPC provider: %d", status)
	}
	log.Printf("Successfully registered RPC provider with handle: %v", regHandle)

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}
	log.Printf("Created activity ID: %v", activityId)

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	// Event data based on samples
	interfaceUuid := GUID{0xff9fd3c4, 0x742e, 0x45e0, [8]byte{0x91, 0xdd, 0x2f, 0x5b, 0xc6, 0x32, 0xa1, 0xdf}}
	typeMgrUuid := GUID{0x00000000, 0x0000, 0x0000, [8]byte{0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00}} // Null GUID
	flags := uint32(0x21)                                                                                    // 33 in decimal
	maxCalls := uint32(1234)                                                                                 // Max calls

	// Security descriptor binary data from sample
	sdHex := "01000480000000000000000000000000140000000200600004000000000314000000001001010000000000051200000000031800000000A00102000000000005200000002102000000031800000000A0010200000000000F020000000100000000031400000000A0010100000000000504000000"
	sdBytes, err := hex.DecodeString(sdHex)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to decode security descriptor hex: %v", err)
	}
	sdSize := uint32(len(sdBytes))
	log.Printf("Security descriptor length: %d bytes", sdSize)
	log.Printf("Security descriptor hex: %s", hex.EncodeToString(sdBytes))

	fmt.Println("Emitting Event ID 14 - FunctionTrace...")
	LogRPCFunctionTraceEvent(regHandle, interfaceUuid, typeMgrUuid, flags, maxCalls, sdSize, sdBytes)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func LogRPCFunctionTraceEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, interfaceUuid GUID, typeMgrUuid GUID, flags uint32, maxCalls uint32, sdSize uint32, sd []byte) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 14
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 0 // Use default channel like sample
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4   // Informational level
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 1  // Start opcode
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x4000000000000000 // 4611686018427387904 from sample

	// Create event data descriptors for all 6 fields as per manifest - simplified approach
	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		// InterfaceUuid (win:GUID)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&interfaceUuid))), Size: 16},
		// TypeMgrUuid (win:GUID)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&typeMgrUuid))), Size: 16},
		// Flags (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&flags))), Size: 4},
		// MaxCalls (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&maxCalls))), Size: 4},
		// SDSize (win:UInt32)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sdSize))), Size: 4},
		// SD (win:Binary)
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&sd[0]))), Size: sdSize},
	}

	log.Printf("EventID: 14")
	log.Printf("EventDescriptor - ID: %d, Level: %d, Channel: %d, Opcode: %d, Keywords: 0x%X",
		eventDescriptor.Id, eventDescriptor.Level, eventDescriptor.Channel, eventDescriptor.Opcode, eventDescriptor.Keyword)
	log.Printf("InterfaceUuid: {%08x-%04x-%04x-%02x%02x-%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x}",
		interfaceUuid.Data1, interfaceUuid.Data2, interfaceUuid.Data3,
		interfaceUuid.Data4[0], interfaceUuid.Data4[1], interfaceUuid.Data4[2], interfaceUuid.Data4[3],
		interfaceUuid.Data4[4], interfaceUuid.Data4[5], interfaceUuid.Data4[6], interfaceUuid.Data4[7])
	log.Printf("TypeMgrUuid: {%08x-%04x-%04x-%02x%02x-%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x}",
		typeMgrUuid.Data1, typeMgrUuid.Data2, typeMgrUuid.Data3,
		typeMgrUuid.Data4[0], typeMgrUuid.Data4[1], typeMgrUuid.Data4[2], typeMgrUuid.Data4[3],
		typeMgrUuid.Data4[4], typeMgrUuid.Data4[5], typeMgrUuid.Data4[6], typeMgrUuid.Data4[7])
	log.Printf("Flags: 0x%X", flags)
	log.Printf("MaxCalls: %d", maxCalls)
	log.Printf("SDSize: %d", sdSize)
	log.Printf("Event data fields count: %d", len(eventData))

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write Microsoft-Windows-RPC function trace event 14: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		log.Printf("Microsoft-Windows-RPC Event 14 (Function trace start) written successfully.")
	}
}
```

`cmd/tcpip.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"os"
	"syscall"
	"unsafe"
)

func LogTcpIpEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, processId uint32, localAddress []byte, remoteAddress []byte, processStartKey uint64, tcb string, verbose bool) {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 1033
	eventDescriptor.Version = 1
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000400000484

	evtStatus := uint32(0)
	compartment := uint32(0)

	tcbUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(tcb)

	localAddressLength := uint32(len(localAddress))
	remoteAddressLength := uint32(len(remoteAddress))

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&localAddressLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(localAddressLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&localAddress[0]))), Size: uint32(len(localAddress))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&remoteAddressLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(remoteAddressLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&remoteAddress[0]))), Size: uint32(len(remoteAddress))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&evtStatus))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(evtStatus))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&compartment))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(compartment))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&tcbUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(tcbUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processStartKey))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processStartKey))},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write TCP/IP event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	}
}

func WriteTcpipEvent(mode string, protocol string) {
	var providerGUID = GUID{0x2f07e2ee, 0x15db, 0x40f1, [8]byte{0x90, 0xef, 0x9d, 0x7b, 0xa2, 0x82, 0x18, 0x8a}}
	var regHandle syscall.Handle

	hr, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&providerGUID)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register provider: %d", hr)
		return
	}

	var amount = 0

	switch mode {
	case "spam":
		amount = 20000
	case "scan":
		amount = rand.Intn(128) + 1
	case "single":
		amount = 1
	}

	for i := 0; i < amount; i++ {
		var rportnumber int

		localAddress := []byte{0x02, 0x00, 0xE7, 0x22, 0x0A, 0xD3, 0x37, 0x15}
		// add 0000000000000000 to make it 16 bytes
		localAddress = append(localAddress, make([]byte, 8)...)

		remoteAddress := []byte{0x02, 0x00, 0xE7, 0x22, 0x0A, 0xD3, 0x37, 0x15}
		// add 0000000000000000 to make it 16 bytes
		remoteAddress = append(remoteAddress, make([]byte, 8)...)

		switch protocol {
		case "random":
			rportnumber = rand.Intn(65534) + 1
			// generate a rancom 16-bit number between 1 and 254 and place it in bit 6
			localAddress[6] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
			localAddress[7] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
			remoteAddress[4] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
			remoteAddress[5] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
		case "kerberos":
			rportnumber = 88
			localAddress[6] = byte(int(42))
			localAddress[7] = byte(int(42))
		case "smb":
			rportnumber = 445
			localAddress[6] = byte(int(42))
			localAddress[7] = byte(int(42))
		}

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())

		lportnumber := rand.Intn(65534) + 1        // Generate a number between 1 and 65534 for the port
		localAddress[2] = byte(lportnumber >> 8)   // High byte
		localAddress[3] = byte(lportnumber & 0xFF) // Low byte

		// 0xE7 and 0x22 represent a 16-bit big-endian number 59170 < port

		remoteAddress[2] = byte(rportnumber >> 8)   // High byte
		remoteAddress[3] = byte(rportnumber & 0xFF) // Low byte
		remoteAddress[6] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
		remoteAddress[7] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)

		localAddressIP := fmt.Sprintf("%d.%d.%d.%d", localAddress[4], localAddress[5], localAddress[6], localAddress[7])
		remoteAddressIP := fmt.Sprintf("%d.%d.%d.%d", remoteAddress[4], remoteAddress[5], remoteAddress[6], remoteAddress[7])

		log.Printf("Sending event %d, LocalAddress: %s:%d > RemoteAddress: %s:%d\n", i, localAddressIP, lportnumber, remoteAddressIP, rportnumber)

		processStartKey := uint64(4222124650660560)
		tcb := "0xFFFFBD0CCEE4E260"

		LogTcpIpEvent(regHandle, processId, localAddress, remoteAddress, processStartKey, tcb, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteInfiniteTcpipEvent() {
	var providerGUID = GUID{0x2f07e2ee, 0x15db, 0x40f1, [8]byte{0x90, 0xef, 0x9d, 0x7b, 0xa2, 0x82, 0x18, 0x8a}}
	var regHandle syscall.Handle

	hr, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&providerGUID)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register provider: %d", hr)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		var rportnumber int
		localAddress := []byte{0x02, 0x00, 0xE7, 0x22, 0x0A, 0xD3, 0x37, 0x15}
		localAddress = append(localAddress, make([]byte, 8)...)

		remoteAddress := []byte{0x02, 0x00, 0xE7, 0x22, 0x0A, 0xD3, 0x37, 0x15}
		remoteAddress = append(remoteAddress, make([]byte, 8)...)

		rportnumber = rand.Intn(65534) + 1
		localAddress[6] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
		localAddress[7] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())

		lportnumber := rand.Intn(65534) + 1
		localAddress[2] = byte(lportnumber >> 8)
		localAddress[3] = byte(lportnumber & 0xFF)

		remoteAddress[2] = byte(rportnumber >> 8)
		remoteAddress[3] = byte(rportnumber & 0xFF)
		remoteAddress[4] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
		remoteAddress[5] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
		remoteAddress[6] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)
		remoteAddress[7] = byte(rand.Intn(254) + 1)

		processStartKey := uint64(4222124650660560)
		tcb := "0xFFFFBD0CCEE4E260"

		success := LogTcpIpEventQuiet(regHandle, processId, localAddress, remoteAddress, processStartKey, tcb)
		UpdateProviderStats("TCP/IP-Network", success)

		count++
	}
}

// LogTcpIpEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogTcpIpEvent for TUI mode
func LogTcpIpEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, processId uint32, localAddress []byte, remoteAddress []byte, processStartKey uint64, tcb string) bool {
	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 1033
	eventDescriptor.Version = 1
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x8000000400000484

	evtStatus := uint32(0)
	compartment := uint32(0)

	tcbUTF16 := syscall.StringToUTF16(tcb)

	localAddressLength := uint32(len(localAddress))
	remoteAddressLength := uint32(len(remoteAddress))

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&localAddressLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(localAddressLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&localAddress[0]))), Size: uint32(len(localAddress))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&remoteAddressLength))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(remoteAddressLength))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&remoteAddress[0]))), Size: uint32(len(remoteAddress))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&evtStatus))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(evtStatus))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&compartment))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(compartment))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&tcbUTF16[0]))), Size: uint32(len(tcbUTF16) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&processStartKey))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(processStartKey))},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return status == 0
}

```

`cmd/wmi.go`:

```go
package cmd

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"
	"math/rand"
	"os"
	"syscall"
	"time"
	"unsafe"
)

var WmiActivityProviderGuid = GUID{0x1418ef04, 0xb0b4, 0x4623, [8]byte{0xbf, 0x7e, 0xd7, 0x4a, 0xb4, 0x7b, 0xbd, 0xaa}}

func WriteRandomWmiEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting WMI Activity events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&WmiActivityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register WMI provider: %d", status)
	}

	for i := 0; i < 100; i++ {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
		creationTime := uint64(time.Now().UnixNano() / 100) // Convert to Windows FILETIME format

		correlationId := fmt.Sprintf("{%08X-%04X-%04X-%02X%02X-%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X}",
			activityId.Data1, activityId.Data2, activityId.Data3,
			activityId.Data4[0], activityId.Data4[1],
			activityId.Data4[2], activityId.Data4[3], activityId.Data4[4], activityId.Data4[5], activityId.Data4[6], activityId.Data4[7])

		className := randomWmiClassName()
		methodName := randomWmiMethodName()
		implementationClass := randomWmiImplementationClass()
		clientMachine := "WORKSTATION-" + randomString(3)
		clientMachineFQDN := clientMachine + ".domain.local"
		user := "DOMAIN\\" + randomString(8)
		namespaceName := randomWmiNamespace()

		LogWmiEvent(regHandle, correlationId, uint32(rand.Intn(1000)), uint32(i), className, methodName,
			implementationClass, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user, processId, creationTime, namespaceName, true, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteWmiEvent() {
	fmt.Println("Emitting WMI Activity events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&WmiActivityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register WMI provider: %d", status)
	}

	var activityId GUID
	hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
	if hr != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
	}

	procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

	processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
	creationTime := uint64(time.Now().UnixNano() / 100) // Convert to Windows FILETIME format

	correlationId := fmt.Sprintf("{%08X-%04X-%04X-%02X%02X-%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X}",
		activityId.Data1, activityId.Data2, activityId.Data3,
		activityId.Data4[0], activityId.Data4[1],
		activityId.Data4[2], activityId.Data4[3], activityId.Data4[4], activityId.Data4[5], activityId.Data4[6], activityId.Data4[7])

	className := "Win32_Process"
	methodName := "Create"
	implementationClass := "CIMWin32"
	clientMachine := "ImInYour"
	clientMachineFQDN := "iminyour.logs.now"
	user := "ARENDEL\\Olaf"
	namespaceName := "root\\cimv2"

	LogWmiEvent(regHandle, correlationId, 1337, 1, className, methodName,
		implementationClass, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user, processId, creationTime, namespaceName, false, 0, true)

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func WriteSuspiciousWmiEvent() {
	log.Println("Emitting suspicious WMI Activity events...")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&WmiActivityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to register WMI provider: %d", status)
	}

	suspiciousActivities := []struct {
		className           string
		methodName          string
		implementationClass string
		namespace           string
		user                string
	}{
		{"Win32_Process", "Create", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "SYSTEM"},
		{"Win32_Service", "Create", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "NT AUTHORITY\\SYSTEM"},
		{"Win32_LogicalDisk", "ChkDsk", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "DOMAIN\\admin"},
		{"Win32_Share", "Create", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "WORKGROUP\\user"},
		{"Win32_ScheduledJob", "Create", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "BUILTIN\\Administrators"},
		{"Win32_ComputerSystem", "JoinDomainOrWorkgroup", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "DOMAIN\\admin"},
		{"Win32_UserAccount", "Create", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "SYSTEM"},
		{"Win32_NetworkAdapter", "Reset", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "NT SERVICE\\NetworkService"},
		{"Win32_Product", "Install", "CIMWin32", "root\\cimv2", "DOMAIN\\serviceaccount"},
		{"Win32_Registry", "SetStringValue", "CIMWin32", "root\\default", "BUILTIN\\Users"},
	}

	for i, activity := range suspiciousActivities {
		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to create GUID: %d", hr)
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
		creationTime := uint64(time.Now().UnixNano() / 100)

		correlationId := fmt.Sprintf("{%08X-%04X-%04X-%02X%02X-%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X}",
			activityId.Data1, activityId.Data2, activityId.Data3,
			activityId.Data4[0], activityId.Data4[1],
			activityId.Data4[2], activityId.Data4[3], activityId.Data4[4], activityId.Data4[5], activityId.Data4[6], activityId.Data4[7])

		clientMachine := "SUSPICIOUS-" + randomString(4)
		clientMachineFQDN := clientMachine + ".evil.corp"

		log.Printf("Emitting suspicious WMI activity: %s.%s", activity.className, activity.methodName)

		LogWmiEvent(regHandle, correlationId, uint32(rand.Intn(9999)), uint32(i), activity.className, activity.methodName,
			activity.implementationClass, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, activity.user, processId, creationTime, activity.namespace, false, i, true)
	}

	procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))
}

func LogWmiEvent(regHandle syscall.Handle, correlationId string, groupOperationId, operationId uint32,
	className, methodName, implementationClass, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user string,
	clientProcessId uint32, clientProcessCreationTime uint64, namespaceName string, isLocal bool, iteration int, verbose bool) {

	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 22 // WMI Activity Event ID
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x4000000000000000 // WMI keyword

	// Convert boolean to byte (0 or 1)
	var isLocalByte byte = 0
	if isLocal {
		isLocalByte = 1
	}

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(correlationId)))), Size: uint32((len(correlationId) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&groupOperationId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(groupOperationId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(operationId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(className)))), Size: uint32((len(className) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(methodName)))), Size: uint32((len(methodName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(implementationClass)))), Size: uint32((len(implementationClass) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(clientMachine)))), Size: uint32((len(clientMachine) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(clientMachineFQDN)))), Size: uint32((len(clientMachineFQDN) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(user)))), Size: uint32((len(user) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientProcessCreationTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientProcessCreationTime))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(namespaceName)))), Size: uint32((len(namespaceName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&isLocalByte))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(isLocalByte))},
	}

	if verbose {
		log.Printf("CorrelationId: %s", correlationId)
		log.Printf("ClassName: %s", className)
		log.Printf("MethodName: %s", methodName)
		log.Printf("User: %s", user)
		log.Printf("NamespaceName: %s", namespaceName)
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write WMI event: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		if verbose {
			if isLocal {
				log.Printf("WMI Event 22 (local) %d written successfully.", iteration)
			} else {
				log.Printf("WMI Event 22 (remote) %d written successfully.", iteration)
			}
		}
	}
}

func randomWmiClassName() string {
	classes := []string{
		"Win32_Process",
		"Win32_Service",
		"Win32_LogicalDisk",
		"Win32_ComputerSystem",
		"Win32_OperatingSystem",
		"Win32_UserAccount",
		"Win32_Share",
		"Win32_NetworkAdapter",
		"Win32_Product",
		"Win32_Registry",
		"Win32_EventLog",
		"Win32_ScheduledJob",
		"Win32_SystemDriver",
		"Win32_PrintJob",
		"Win32_SecurityCenter",
	}
	return classes[rand.Intn(len(classes))]
}

func randomWmiMethodName() string {
	methods := []string{
		"Create",
		"Delete",
		"Modify",
		"Start",
		"Stop",
		"Pause",
		"Resume",
		"Terminate",
		"Reset",
		"Install",
		"Uninstall",
		"Configure",
		"GetSecurityDescriptor",
		"SetSecurityDescriptor",
		"ExecQuery",
	}
	return methods[rand.Intn(len(methods))]
}

func randomWmiImplementationClass() string {
	implementations := []string{
		"CIMWin32",
		"Win32Provider",
		"CIMProvider",
		"WMIProvider",
		"SystemProvider",
	}
	return implementations[rand.Intn(len(implementations))]
}

func randomWmiNamespace() string {
	namespaces := []string{
		"root\\cimv2",
		"root\\default",
		"root\\security",
		"root\\wmi",
		"root\\microsoft\\windows\\defender",
		"root\\subscription",
		"root\\policy",
		"root\\standardcimv2",
		"root\\rsop",
		"root\\interop",
		"root\\cimv2\\security",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender\\antivirus",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender\\antivirus\\scan",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender\\antivirus\\scan\\history",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender\\antivirus\\scan\\history\\last",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender\\antivirus\\scan\\history\\last\\1",
		"root\\cimv2\\security\\microsoft\\windows\\defender\\antivirus\\scan\\history\\last\\2",
	}
	return namespaces[rand.Intn(len(namespaces))]
}

func LogWmiEvent11(regHandle syscall.Handle, correlationId string, groupOperationId, operationId uint32,
	operation, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user string,
	clientProcessId uint32, clientProcessCreationTime uint64, namespaceName string, isLocal bool, iteration int, verbose bool) {

	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 11 // WMI Activity Event ID 11
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16 // Operational channel
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4    // Informational
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x4000000000000000 // WMI keyword

	// Convert boolean to byte (0 or 1)
	var isLocalByte byte = 0
	if isLocal {
		isLocalByte = 1
	}

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(correlationId)))), Size: uint32((len(correlationId) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&groupOperationId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(groupOperationId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(operationId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(operation)))), Size: uint32((len(operation) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(clientMachine)))), Size: uint32((len(clientMachine) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(clientMachineFQDN)))), Size: uint32((len(clientMachineFQDN) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(user)))), Size: uint32((len(user) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientProcessCreationTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientProcessCreationTime))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(namespaceName)))), Size: uint32((len(namespaceName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&isLocalByte))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(isLocalByte))},
	}

	if verbose {
		log.Printf("CorrelationId: %s", correlationId)
		log.Printf("Operation: %s", operation)
		log.Printf("User: %s", user)
		log.Printf("NamespaceName: %s", namespaceName)
		log.Printf("IsLocal: %t", isLocal)
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to write WMI event 11: %s", GetWindowsErrorDescription(uint32(status)))
		return
	} else {
		if verbose {
			log.Printf("WMI Event 11 %d written successfully.", iteration)
		}
	}
}

func randomWmiOperation() string {
	operations := []string{
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_Process",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_Service",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_ComputerSystem",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_OperatingSystem",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_UserAccount",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_Share",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_NetworkAdapter",
		"IWbemServices::ExecQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_LogicalDisk",
		"IWbemServices::CreateInstanceEnum - Win32_Process",
		"IWbemServices::CreateInstanceEnum - Win32_Service",
		"IWbemServices::CreateInstanceEnum - Win32_ComputerSystem",
		"IWbemServices::GetObject - Win32_Process",
		"IWbemServices::GetObject - Win32_Service",
		"IWbemServices::PutInstance - Win32_Process",
		"IWbemServices::DeleteInstance - Win32_Process",
		"IWbemServices::ExecMethod - Win32_Process.Create",
		"IWbemServices::ExecMethod - Win32_Service.StartService",
		"IWbemServices::ExecMethod - Win32_Service.StopService",
		"IWbemServices::ExecNotificationQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_ProcessStartTrace",
		"IWbemServices::ExecNotificationQuery - SELECT * FROM Win32_ProcessStopTrace",
	}
	return operations[rand.Intn(len(operations))]
}

func WriteInfiniteRandomWmiEvent() {
	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&WmiActivityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register WMI provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			break
		}

		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			UpdateProviderStats("WMI-Activity", false)
			continue
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
		creationTime := uint64(time.Now().UnixNano() / 100)

		correlationId := fmt.Sprintf("{%08X-%04X-%04X-%02X%02X-%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X}",
			activityId.Data1, activityId.Data2, activityId.Data3,
			activityId.Data4[0], activityId.Data4[1],
			activityId.Data4[2], activityId.Data4[3], activityId.Data4[4], activityId.Data4[5], activityId.Data4[6], activityId.Data4[7])

		className := randomWmiClassName()
		methodName := randomWmiMethodName()
		implementationClass := randomWmiImplementationClass()
		clientMachine := "ImInYour-" + randomString(3)
		clientMachineFQDN := clientMachine + ".domain.local"
		user := "DOMAIN\\" + randomString(8)
		namespaceName := randomWmiNamespace()

		success := LogWmiEventQuiet(regHandle, correlationId, uint32(rand.Intn(1000)), uint32(count), className, methodName,
			implementationClass, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user, processId, creationTime, namespaceName, true, count)
		UpdateProviderStats("WMI-Activity", success)

		count++
	}
}

// LogWmiEventQuiet is a quiet version of LogWmiEvent for TUI mode
func LogWmiEventQuiet(regHandle syscall.Handle, correlationId string, groupOperationId, operationId uint32,
	className, methodName, implementationClass, clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user string,
	clientProcessId uint32, clientProcessCreationTime uint64, namespaceName string, isLocal bool, iteration int) bool {

	var eventDescriptor EventDescriptor
	eventDescriptor.Id = 5
	eventDescriptor.Version = 0
	eventDescriptor.Channel = 16
	eventDescriptor.Level = 4
	eventDescriptor.Opcode = 0
	eventDescriptor.Task = 0
	eventDescriptor.Keyword = 0x4000000000000000

	// Convert boolean to byte (0 or 1)
	var isLocalByte byte = 0
	if isLocal {
		isLocalByte = 1
	}

	eventData := []EventDataDescriptor{
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(correlationId)))), Size: uint32((len(correlationId) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&groupOperationId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(groupOperationId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&operationId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(operationId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(className)))), Size: uint32((len(className) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(methodName)))), Size: uint32((len(methodName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(implementationClass)))), Size: uint32((len(implementationClass) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(clientMachine)))), Size: uint32((len(clientMachine) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(clientMachineFQDN)))), Size: uint32((len(clientMachineFQDN) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(user)))), Size: uint32((len(user) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientProcessId))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientProcessId))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&clientProcessCreationTime))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(clientProcessCreationTime))},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(syscall.StringToUTF16Ptr(namespaceName)))), Size: uint32((len(namespaceName) + 1) * 2)},
		{Ptr: uint64(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&isLocalByte))), Size: uint32(unsafe.Sizeof(isLocalByte))},
	}

	status, _, _ := procEventWrite.Call(uintptr(regHandle), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventDescriptor)), uintptr(len(eventData)), uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&eventData[0])))
	return status == 0
}

func WriteInfiniteRandomWmiEvent11() {
	log.Println("Starting infinite WMI Activity Event 11 events... Press ESC to stop")

	var regHandle syscall.Handle
	status, _, _ := procEventRegister.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&WmiActivityProviderGuid)), 0, 0, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&regHandle)))
	if status != 0 {
		log.Printf("Failed to register WMI provider: %d", status)
		return
	}
	defer procEventUnregister.Call(uintptr(regHandle))

	count := 0
	for {
		if IsEscapePressed() {
			log.Printf("Escape pressed. Sent %d WMI Event 11s.", count)
			break
		}

		var activityId GUID
		hr, _, _ := procCoCreateGuid.Call(uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))
		if hr != 0 {
			log.Printf("Failed to create GUID: %d, continuing...", hr)
			continue
		}

		procEventActivityId.Call(3, uintptr(unsafe.Pointer(&activityId)))

		processId := uint32(os.Getpid())
		creationTime := uint64(time.Now().UnixNano() / 100)

		correlationId := fmt.Sprintf("{%08X-%04X-%04X-%02X%02X-%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X}",
			activityId.Data1, activityId.Data2, activityId.Data3,
			activityId.Data4[0], activityId.Data4[1],
			activityId.Data4[2], activityId.Data4[3], activityId.Data4[4], activityId.Data4[5], activityId.Data4[6], activityId.Data4[7])

		operation := randomWmiOperation()
		clientMachine := "ImInYour-" + randomString(3)
		clientMachineFQDN := clientMachine + ".logs.now"
		user := "ARENDEL\\" + randomString(8)
		namespaceName := randomWmiNamespace()
		isLocal := rand.Intn(2) == 1

		LogWmiEvent11(regHandle, correlationId, uint32(rand.Intn(1000)), uint32(count), operation,
			clientMachine, clientMachineFQDN, user, processId, creationTime, namespaceName, isLocal, count, false)

		count++
		// if count%100 == 0 {
		// 	log.Printf("Sent %d WMI Event 11s...", count)
		// }
	}
}
```

`internal/antimalware.go`:

```go
package internal

// obfuscation key for XOR encoding - can be any random value
const obfuscationKey = 0x5A

// obfuscate encodes a string using XOR to hide it from binary analysis
func obfuscate(s string) string {
	result := make([]byte, len(s))
	for i, b := range []byte(s) {
		result[i] = b ^ obfuscationKey
	}
	return string(result)
}

// deobfuscate decodes an XOR-encoded string
func deobfuscate(s string) string {
	result := make([]byte, len(s))
	for i, b := range []byte(s) {
		result[i] = b ^ obfuscationKey
	}
	return string(result)
}

type ThreatData struct {
	ThreatName    string // This will be stored obfuscated
	DetectionGuid string
	RealPath      string
	Sha1          string
}

// GetThreatName returns the deobfuscated threat name
func (t *ThreatData) GetThreatName() string {
	return deobfuscate(t.ThreatName)
}

// List of known threats to be used in the antimalware module
var ThreatDataList = []ThreatData{
	{"\x0c3(\x0e556`\r34ihu\x08?75.?\x08?=\x123,?\x195*#t\x18", "ffd347f7-88fc-79b7-db59-b322429dd6f3", "C:\\Windows\\System32\\dpsVtevO.tmp", "2f9973ab4886b37964a449da52b45ea0cc49fef2"},
	{"\x18?2;,35(`\r34ihu\x08?75.?\x08?=\x1e/7*t\x1b", "602b2c85-41a6-5bf5-357b-bf073865b9fc", "C:\\Windows\\System32\\kMNyWtTS.tmp", "02df4cbac806d14c9151d9be87670398f78825aa"},

// lists created with this kql
// DeviceEvents
// | where ActionType contains "AntivirusDetection"
// | extend ThreatName=tostring(parse_json(AdditionalFields).ThreatName)
// | extend DetectionGuid=tostring(parse_json(AdditionalFields).DetectionGuid)
// | where not(isempty(DetectionGuid))
// | where not(ThreatName has_any ("Hacktool","Virus","PWS","Backdoor","Exploit","Ransom","TrojanDropper","BrowserModifier","Worm","Trojan"))
// | where not(ThreatName has_any ("EUS","TrojanDownloader","VirTool","TrojanSpy","DoS", "TrojanClicker", "Behavior"))
// // | where ThreatName !in~ ("Worm:AutoIt/Victy!rfn","Trojan:O97M/Sadoca.C!ml","Trojan:Script/Phonzy.A!ml","Trojan:VBA/AgentTesla.GC!MTB","Trojan:Script/Wacatac.B!ml")
// | distinct ThreatName, DetectionGuid, SHA1
// | extend Separator="c:\\ImInYourLogs\\BamboozlEDR\\"
// | extend fakefilename = strcat("file_", tostring(toint(rand()*100000))) // Generate random filename
// | extend realPath=strcat(Separator, fakefilename, ".exe") // Append file extension
// | project ThreatName, DetectionGuid, SHA1, realPath
// | take 3000
```

`internal/etw.go`:

```go
package internal

import (
	"fmt"

	"github.com/Microsoft/go-winio/pkg/etw"
	"github.com/google/uuid"
)

// GenerateUUID generates a new UUID string
func GenerateUUID() string {
	return uuid.New().String()
}

// WriteETWEvent writes an event to the specified ETW provider
func WriteETWEvent(providerGUID, providerName, eventMetadata, events string, sequenceNumber int) error {
	// Create a new provider
	provider, err := etw.NewProvider(providerName, nil)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to create provider: %v", err)
	}
	defer provider.Close()

	// Write the event
	err = provider.WriteEvent(
		// "CyberSecurityEvent", // Message string
		"CyberSecurity", // Message string
		etw.WithEventOpts(etw.WithLevel(etw.LevelInfo)),
		etw.WithFields(
			etw.StringField("EventMetadata", eventMetadata),
			etw.Uint8Field("IsEventCompressed", 0),
			etw.StringField("PartA_iKey", "P-WDATP"),
			etw.Uint32Field("SenseEpoch", 2897472),
			etw.Uint32Field("SenseSeqNum", uint32(sequenceNumber)),
			etw.StringField("events", events),
			// etw.StringField("id", GenerateUUID()),
			etw.StringField("id", "32623739663636652D623439612D346631322D623538632D65666162323861333463613400623065303963363165666237373966613664613537616130383539663265653137303930373165640031302E383739322E32363130302E333737350031323931393237362D663833362D346635362D613738382D3030623337343864343132330036336666636633312D353135382D343837332D396166612D34303530653562363439353600630075007000630061006B006500000065393539636531372D303965622D343662652D623239302D30303534663363656162356100005B5D00640C0400000000000C00"),
		),
	)
	if err != nil {
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to write event: %v", err)
	}

	return nil
}

```

`main.go`:

```go
package main

import (
	"bamboozlEDR/cmd"
	"bamboozlEDR/internal"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"log"
	"strings"
	"sync"
	"time"

	"github.com/charmbracelet/bubbles/key"
	"github.com/charmbracelet/bubbles/list"
	"github.com/charmbracelet/bubbles/viewport"
	tea "github.com/charmbracelet/bubbletea"
	"github.com/charmbracelet/lipgloss"
)

// Styles
var (
	titleStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().
			BorderStyle(lipgloss.RoundedBorder()).
			BorderForeground(lipgloss.Color("#33658A")).
			Padding(0, 1).
			Bold(true)

	menuStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().
			BorderStyle(lipgloss.RoundedBorder()).
			BorderForeground(lipgloss.Color("#33658A")).
			Padding(1, 2)

	logStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().
			BorderStyle(lipgloss.RoundedBorder()).
			BorderForeground(lipgloss.Color("#3B4252")).
			Padding(1, 2)

	statusStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().
			BorderStyle(lipgloss.RoundedBorder()).
			BorderForeground(lipgloss.Color("205")).
			Padding(0, 1)

	selectedItemStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().
				Foreground(lipgloss.Color("#65C4FF")).
				Bold(true)

	helpStyle = lipgloss.NewStyle().
			Foreground(lipgloss.Color("241"))
)

// Menu items
type menuItem struct {
	title   string
	value   string
	desc    string
	submenu []menuItem
}

func (i menuItem) FilterValue() string { return i.title }

// List item delegate
type itemDelegate struct{}

func (d itemDelegate) Height() int                             { return 1 }
func (d itemDelegate) Spacing() int                            { return 0 }
func (d itemDelegate) Update(_ tea.Msg, _ *list.Model) tea.Cmd { return nil }
func (d itemDelegate) Render(w io.Writer, m list.Model, index int, item list.Item) {
	i, ok := item.(menuItem)
	if !ok {
		return
	}

	// Check if this item is selected
	isSelected := index == m.Index()

	str := fmt.Sprintf("%s", i.title)
	if i.desc != "" {
		str += lipgloss.NewStyle().Foreground(lipgloss.Color("241")).Render(" - " + i.desc)
	}

	// Apply selection styling
	if isSelected {
		str = selectedItemStyle.Render("â–¶ " + str)
	} else {
		str = "  " + str
	}

	fmt.Fprint(w, str)
}

// Application state
type appState int

const (
	stateMainMenu appState = iota
	stateSubMenu
	stateRunning
	stateBufferOverflow
)

// Model for the TUI application
type model struct {
	state           appState
	mainList        list.Model
	subList         list.Model
	viewport        viewport.Model
	logs            []string
	stats           string
	currentProvider string
	subProvider     string
	width           int
	height          int
	isRunning       bool
	stopFunc        func()
	keys            keyMap
}

// Key map
type keyMap struct {
	Up    key.Binding
	Down  key.Binding
	Enter key.Binding
	Back  key.Binding
	Quit  key.Binding
	Help  key.Binding
}

func newKeyMap() keyMap {
	return keyMap{
		Up: key.NewBinding(
			key.WithKeys("up", "k"),
			key.WithHelp("â†‘/k", "move up"),
		),
		Down: key.NewBinding(
			key.WithKeys("down", "j"),
			key.WithHelp("â†“/j", "move down"),
		),
		Enter: key.NewBinding(
			key.WithKeys("enter"),
			key.WithHelp("enter", "select"),
		),
		Back: key.NewBinding(
			key.WithKeys("esc", "backspace"),
			key.WithHelp("esc", "back/stop"),
		),
		Quit: key.NewBinding(
			key.WithKeys("ctrl+c", "q"),
			key.WithHelp("q", "quit"),
		),
		Help: key.NewBinding(
			key.WithKeys("?"),
			key.WithHelp("?", "toggle help"),
		),
	}
}

// Initialize the model
func initialModel() model {
	// Create main menu items
	mainMenuItems := createMainMenuItems()

	// Create main list
	mainList := list.New(mainMenuItems, itemDelegate{}, 0, 0)
	mainList.Title = "Select ETW Provider"
	mainList.SetShowStatusBar(false)
	mainList.SetFilteringEnabled(false)
	mainList.Styles.Title = titleStyle

	// Create sub list
	subList := list.New([]list.Item{}, itemDelegate{}, 0, 0)
	subList.SetShowStatusBar(false)
	subList.SetFilteringEnabled(false)
	subList.Styles.Title = titleStyle

	// Create viewport for logs
	vp := viewport.New(0, 0)

	// Initialize with welcome messages
	initialLogs := []string{
		fmt.Sprintf("[%s] ðŸ›¡ï¸  BamboozlEDR TUI Started", time.Now().Format("15:04:05")),
		fmt.Sprintf("[%s] Navigate with â†‘/â†“, select with Enter, ESC to go back, q to quit", time.Now().Format("15:04:05")),
		fmt.Sprintf("[%s] Select a provider from the menu to generate ETW events", time.Now().Format("15:04:05")),
	}
	vp.SetContent(strings.Join(initialLogs, "\n"))

	return model{
		state:           stateMainMenu,
		mainList:        mainList,
		subList:         subList,
		viewport:        vp,
		logs:            initialLogs,
		currentProvider: "",
		subProvider:     "",
		keys:            newKeyMap(),
	}
}

// Create main menu items (now dynamic to reflect ETW session state)
func createMainMenuItems() []list.Item {
	items := []list.Item{
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP",
			value:   "antimalwarertp",
			desc:    "Generate real-time protection events",
			submenu: getAntimalwareRTPSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-AMSI",
			value:   "amsi",
			desc:    "Generate AMSI provider events",
			submenu: getAmsiSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-Antimalware",
			value:   "antimalware",
			desc:    "Generate antimalware detection events",
			submenu: getAntimalwareSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-AppLocker",
			value:   "applocker",
			desc:    "Generate AppLocker events",
			submenu: getAppLockerSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-CodeIntegrity",
			value:   "codeintegrity",
			desc:    "Generate Code Integrity events",
			submenu: getCodeIntegritySubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-Crypto-DPAPI-Events",
			value:   "DPAPI",
			desc:    "Generate DPAPI access events",
			submenu: getDpapiSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-DotNETRuntime",
			value:   "dotnet",
			desc:    "Generate .NET runtime events",
			submenu: getDotnetSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-Ldap-Client",
			value:   "ldapclient",
			desc:    "Generate LDAP client events",
			submenu: getLdapSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-NTLM",
			value:   "ntlm",
			desc:    "Generate NTLM blocking events",
			submenu: getNTLMSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-PowerShell",
			value:   "powershell",
			desc:    "Generate PowerShell events",
			submenu: getPowerShellSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-RPC",
			value:   "rpc",
			desc:    "Generate RPC function trace events",
			submenu: getRPCSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-TCPIP",
			value:   "tcpip",
			desc:    "Generate TCP/IP network events",
			submenu: getTcpipSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-WMI-Activity",
			value:   "wmiactivity",
			desc:    "Generate WMI activity events",
			submenu: getWmiSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title:   "Microsoft-Windows-Windows Defender",
			value:   "defender",
			desc:    "Generate Windows Defender events",
			submenu: getDefenderSubmenu(),
		},
		menuItem{
			title: "Cyber events",
			value: "cyberevents",
			desc:  "Inject data into MDE trace session - No impact on EDR",
		},
		menuItem{
			title: "BamboozlEDR",
			value: "bamboozle",
			desc:  "Execute multiple events to confuse EDR",
		},
		menuItem{
			title: "Buffer Overflow",
			value: "bufferoverflow",
			desc:  "Generate unlimited events from all providers",
		},
	}

	// Only add ETW Trace Monitor option if running as administrator
	if cmd.IsRunningAsAdmin() {
		etwTitle, etwDesc := cmd.GetETWTraceMenuInfo()
		items = append(items, menuItem{
			title: etwTitle,
			value: "etwtraces",
			desc:  etwDesc,
		})
	}

	// Always add Exit option last
	items = append(items, menuItem{
		title: "Exit",
		value: "exit",
		desc:  "Exit the application",
	})

	return items
}

		{title: "Ransomware", value: "ransomware", desc: "Generate ransomware detection"},

	}
}
```
