// wrapText wraps text to fit within a specified width
func wrapText(text string, width int) string {
	if width <= 0 {
		return text
	}

	lines := strings.Split(text, "\n")
	var wrappedLines []string

	for _, line := range lines {
		if len(line) <= width {
			wrappedLines = append(wrappedLines, line)
			continue
		}

		// Split long lines
		words := strings.Fields(line)
		if len(words) == 0 {
			wrappedLines = append(wrappedLines, line)
			continue
		}

		currentLine := ""
		for _, word := range words {
			// If adding this word would exceed width, start a new line
			if len(currentLine)+len(word)+1 > width && currentLine != "" {
				wrappedLines = append(wrappedLines, currentLine)
				currentLine = word
			} else {
				if currentLine == "" {
					currentLine = word
				} else {
					currentLine += " " + word
				}
			}
		}
		if currentLine != "" {
			wrappedLines = append(wrappedLines, currentLine)
		}
	}

	return strings.Join(wrappedLines, "\n")
}

// Messages for TUI updates
type logMsg string
type statsMsg string
type finishedMsg struct{}
type actionCompleteMsg struct{}

// Init function (required by tea.Model interface)
func (m model) Init() tea.Cmd {
	return nil
}

// Update function
func (m model) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
	var cmd tea.Cmd
	var cmds []tea.Cmd

	switch msg := msg.(type) {
	case tea.WindowSizeMsg:
		m.width = msg.Width
		m.height = msg.Height

		// Resize components
		listHeight := m.height - 10
		logHeight := m.height - 10
		listWidth := m.width/2 - 4
		logWidth := m.width/2 - 4

		m.mainList.SetSize(listWidth, listHeight)
		m.subList.SetSize(listWidth, listHeight)
		m.viewport.Width = logWidth
		m.viewport.Height = logHeight

	case tea.KeyMsg:
		// Handle ESC explicitly first, before list components can process it
		if msg.String() == "esc" {
			if m.state == stateRunning || m.state == stateBufferOverflow {
				// Stop running process
				if m.isRunning && m.stopFunc != nil {
					m.stopFunc()
				}
				m.isRunning = false
				m.state = stateMainMenu
				m.addLog("Process stopped.")
				return m, nil
			} else if m.state == stateSubMenu {
				m.state = stateMainMenu
				return m, nil
			} else if m.state == stateMainMenu {
				// At main menu, ESC does nothing - show help message
				m.addLog("ðŸ’¡ Use 'q' to quit the application, or select 'Exit' from the menu")
				return m, nil
			}
		}

		switch {
		case key.Matches(msg, m.keys.Quit):
			if m.isRunning && m.stopFunc != nil {
				m.stopFunc()
			}
			return m, tea.Quit

		case key.Matches(msg, m.keys.Enter):
			if m.state == stateMainMenu {
				item := m.mainList.SelectedItem().(menuItem)
				if item.value == "exit" {
					return m, tea.Quit
				}

				if len(item.submenu) > 0 {
					// Has submenu
					subItems := make([]list.Item, len(item.submenu))
					for i, sub := range item.submenu {
						subItems[i] = sub
					}
					m.subList.SetItems(subItems)
					m.subList.Title = "Choose " + item.title + " Option"
					m.currentProvider = item.value
					m.state = stateSubMenu
				} else {
					// Direct action
					m.currentProvider = item.value
					m.subProvider = ""
					cmd = m.executeAction()
					cmds = append(cmds, cmd)
				}
			} else if m.state == stateSubMenu {
				item := m.subList.SelectedItem().(menuItem)
				if item.value == "back" {
					m.state = stateMainMenu
				} else {
					m.subProvider = item.value
					cmd = m.executeAction()
					cmds = append(cmds, cmd)
				}
			}
		}

	case logMsg:
		m.addLog(string(msg))

	case statsMsg:
		m.stats = string(msg)

	case finishedMsg:
		m.isRunning = false
		if m.state == stateBufferOverflow {
			m.state = stateMainMenu
		} else {
			m.state = stateMainMenu
		}
		m.addLog("Process completed.")

	case actionCompleteMsg:
		// Action completed
		m.isRunning = false
		m.state = stateMainMenu

		// Refresh main menu if ETW trace session was toggled
		if m.currentProvider == "etwtraces" {
			m.refreshMainMenu()
		}

		m.addLog("Action completed. Returning to main menu.")
		return m, nil
	}

	// Update components based on state
	switch m.state {
	case stateMainMenu:
		m.mainList, cmd = m.mainList.Update(msg)
		cmds = append(cmds, cmd)
	case stateSubMenu:
		m.subList, cmd = m.subList.Update(msg)
		cmds = append(cmds, cmd)
	}

	// Update viewport only with appropriate keys (Page Up/Down, not arrow keys)
	if keyMsg, ok := msg.(tea.KeyMsg); ok {
		// Only allow Page Up/Page Down and other non-navigation keys to reach viewport
		switch keyMsg.String() {
		case "up", "down", "k", "j":
			// Don't pass arrow keys to viewport - they're for menu navigation only
		case "pgup", "pgdown", "home", "end":
			// Allow page navigation keys to scroll logs
			m.viewport, cmd = m.viewport.Update(msg)
			cmds = append(cmds, cmd)
		}
	} else {
		// Pass non-key messages to viewport (resize, etc.)
		m.viewport, cmd = m.viewport.Update(msg)
		cmds = append(cmds, cmd)
	}

	return m, tea.Batch(cmds...)
}

// Add log message and auto-scroll
func (m *model) addLog(msg string) {
	timestamp := time.Now().Format("15:04:05")
	logLine := fmt.Sprintf("[%s] %s", timestamp, msg)
	m.logs = append(m.logs, logLine)

	// Keep only last 1000 log lines
	if len(m.logs) > 1000 {
		m.logs = m.logs[len(m.logs)-1000:]
	}

	// Update viewport content with text wrapping
	content := strings.Join(m.logs, "\n")
	wrappedContent := wrapText(content, m.viewport.Width-2) // -2 for padding
	m.viewport.SetContent(wrappedContent)
	m.viewport.GotoBottom()
}

// Execute the selected action
func (m *model) executeAction() tea.Cmd {
	if m.currentProvider == "bufferoverflow" {
		m.state = stateBufferOverflow
		m.addLog("ðŸš€ Starting Buffer Overflow - maximum throughput mode...")
		m.addLog("Initializing all ETW providers...")
		m.isRunning = true
		return tea.Cmd(func() tea.Msg {
			m.runBufferOverflow()
			return actionCompleteMsg{}
		})
	} else if m.currentProvider == "bamboozle" {
		m.state = stateRunning
		m.addLog("ðŸŽ¯ Starting BamboozlEDR - parallel spam mode...")
		m.addLog("Executing multiple ETW providers simultaneously...")
		m.isRunning = true
		return tea.Cmd(func() tea.Msg {
			m.runBamboozle()
			return actionCompleteMsg{}
		})
	} else {
		m.state = stateRunning
		m.addLog(fmt.Sprintf("â–¶ï¸  Executing: %s", m.getActionDescription()))
		m.isRunning = true
		return tea.Cmd(func() tea.Msg {
			m.runAction()
			return actionCompleteMsg{}
		})
	}
}

// Get description of current action
func (m *model) getActionDescription() string {
	if m.subProvider != "" {
		return fmt.Sprintf("%s - %s", m.currentProvider, m.subProvider)
	}
	return m.currentProvider
}

// refreshMainMenu updates the main menu with current ETW session state
func (m *model) refreshMainMenu() {
	// Get updated menu items
	updatedItems := createMainMenuItems()

	// Update the main list with new items
	m.mainList.SetItems(updatedItems)

	m.addLog("Menu refreshed to reflect ETW session state")
}

// Run buffer overflow mode
func (m *model) runBufferOverflow() {
	// Initialize systems
	cmd.InitializeProviderStats()
	cmd.InitializeGuidPool(100000)

	m.addLog("Initializing advanced performance optimizations...")
	m.addLog("Press ESC to stop all infinite spam functions")

	// Set stop function
	stopChan := make(chan bool)
	m.stopFunc = func() {
		close(stopChan)
	}

	var wg sync.WaitGroup
	wg.Add(11) // Added one more for stats updater, DPAPI, PowerShell, CodeIntegrity, and AppLocker

	// Start stats updater goroutine
	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		ticker := time.NewTicker(2 * time.Second)
		defer ticker.Stop()

		for {
			select {
			case <-ticker.C:
				statsTable := cmd.GetProviderStatsTable()
				// Send stats to TUI (this will be handled in Update function)
				go func() {
					if logWriter, ok := log.Writer().(*logWriter); ok && logWriter.program != nil {
						logWriter.program.Send(statsMsg(statsTable))
					}
				}()
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			}
		}
	}()

	// Start all spam functions
	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteAntimalwareEvent("threat")
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteAntimalwareEvent("benign")
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomLdapEventOriginal()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteTcpipEvent()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomWmiEvent()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomAmsiEvent()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteDPAPIEvent()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomPowerShellEvent()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomCodeIntegrityEvents()
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomAppLockerEvents()
			}
		}
	}()

	wg.Wait()
}

// Run bamboozle mode - parallel spam functions
func (m *model) runBamboozle() {
	m.addLog("ðŸŽ¯ Bamboozling the EDR with parallel spam attacks...")
	m.addLog("Press ESC to stop all spam functions")

	// Set stop function
	stopChan := make(chan bool)
	m.stopFunc = func() {
		close(stopChan)
	}

	var wg sync.WaitGroup
	wg.Add(7) // Seven spam functions running in parallel (added DPAPI, PowerShell, CodeIntegrity, and AppLocker)

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸŒ Generating LDAP search events...")
				cmd.WriteRandomLdapEvent()
				log.Println("LDAP events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸŒ Generating TCP/IP network events...")
				cmd.WriteTcpipEvent("spam", "random")
				log.Println("TCP/IP events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸ¦  Generating antimalware threat events...")
				cmd.WriteAntimalwareEvent("threat")
				log.Println("Antimalware threat events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸ” Generating DPAPI events...")
				cmd.WriteSpamDPAPIEvent()
				log.Println("DPAPI events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸŸ¦ Generating PowerShell events...")
				cmd.WriteRandomPowerShellEvent()
				log.Println("PowerShell events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸ›¡ï¸ Generating CodeIntegrity events...")
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomCodeIntegrityEvents()
				log.Println("CodeIntegrity events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	go func() {
		defer wg.Done()
		for {
			select {
			case <-stopChan:
				return
			default:
				log.Println("ðŸ”’ Generating AppLocker events...")
				cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomAppLockerEvents()
				log.Println("AppLocker events generated successfully")
				time.Sleep(10 * time.Millisecond)
			}
		}
	}()

	m.addLog("ðŸŽ­ Bamboozled the EDR - running parallel spam to multiple providers")
	m.addLog("ðŸ“Š Multiple ETW providers hitting capping limits simultaneously...")

	wg.Wait()
}

// Run regular action
func (m *model) runAction() {
	// Action completion is now handled by actionCompleteMsg

	switch m.currentProvider {
	case "antimalware":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "randommalware":
			log.Println("Generating random malware detection event...")
			cmd.WriteAntimalwareEvent("random")
			log.Println("Random malware event generated successfully")
		case "randombenign":
			log.Println("Generating random benign detection event...")
			cmd.WriteAntimalwareEvent("randombenign")
			log.Println("Random benign event generated successfully")
		case "spamantimalware":
			log.Println("Generating malware threat detection events...")
			cmd.WriteAntimalwareEvent("threat")
			log.Println("Malware threat events generated successfully")
		case "spambenign":
			log.Println("Generating benign detection events...")
			cmd.WriteAntimalwareEvent("benign")
			log.Println("Benign events generated successfully")
		case "ransomware":
			log.Println("Generating ransomware detection event...")
			cmd.WriteAntimalwareEvent("ransom")
			log.Println("Ransomware event generated successfully")
		}
	case "antimalwarertp":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "antimalwarertp-detection":
			log.Println("Generating Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP detection events...")
			cmd.WriteAntimalwareRTPDetectionEvent()
			log.Println("Microsoft-Antimalware-RTP detection events generated successfully")
		}
	case "rpc":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "rpc-functiontrace":
			log.Println("Generating Microsoft-Windows-RPC function trace event...")
			cmd.WriteRPCFunctionTraceEvent()
			log.Println("Microsoft-Windows-RPC function trace event generated successfully")
		}
	case "DPAPI":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "dpapi":
			log.Println("Generating single DPAPI access event...")
			cmd.WriteDPAPIEvent()
			log.Println("DPAPI event generated successfully")
		case "spamdpapi":
			log.Println("Generating multiple DPAPI events...")
			cmd.WriteSpamDPAPIEvent()
			log.Println("DPAPI spam events generated successfully")
		case "infinitedpapi":
			log.Println("Generating infinite DPAPI events...")
			cmd.WriteInfiniteDPAPIEvent()
			log.Println("DPAPI infinite events completed")
		}
	case "ldapclient":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "ldap":
			log.Println("Generating ADExplorer LDAP search event...")
			cmd.WriteLdapEvent()
			log.Println("LDAP event generated successfully")
		case "sharphoundldap":
			log.Println("Generating SharpHound LDAP search events...")
			cmd.WriteSharpHoundLdapEvent()
			log.Println("SharpHound LDAP events generated successfully")
		case "randomldap":
			log.Println("Generating random LDAP search events...")
			cmd.WriteRandomLdapEvent()
			log.Println("Random LDAP events generated successfully")
		}
	case "tcpip":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "tcpipspam":
			cmd.WriteTcpipEvent("spam", "random")
		case "tcpsmbscan":
			cmd.WriteTcpipEvent("scan", "smb")
		case "tcpipsingle":
			cmd.WriteTcpipEvent("single", "random")
		case "tcpipkerberos":
			cmd.WriteTcpipEvent("single", "kerberos")
		case "tcpipsmb":
			cmd.WriteTcpipEvent("single", "smb")
		}
	case "wmiactivity":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "wmi":
			cmd.WriteWmiEvent()
		case "suspiciouswmi":
			cmd.WriteSuspiciousWmiEvent()
		case "randomwmi":
			cmd.WriteRandomWmiEvent()
		case "wmi11":
			cmd.WriteWmiEvent11()
		case "suspiciouswmi11":
			cmd.WriteSuspiciousWmiEvent11()
		case "randomwmi11":
			cmd.WriteRandomWmiEvent11()
		case "localwmi11":
			cmd.WriteLocalWmiEvent11()
		case "remotewmi11":
			cmd.WriteRemoteWmiEvent11()
		}
	case "amsi":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "amsi":
			cmd.WriteAmsiEvent()
		case "suspiciousamsi":
			cmd.WriteSuspiciousAmsiEvent()
		case "randomamsi":
			cmd.WriteRandomAmsiEvent()
		}
	case "powershell":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "powershellsingle":
			log.Println("Generating single random PowerShell event...")
			cmd.WriteRandomSinglePowerShellEvent()
			log.Println("PowerShell event generated successfully")
		case "powershellamsi":
			log.Println("Generating random PowerShell AMSI event...")
			cmd.WriteRandomSinglePowerShellAmsiEvent()
			log.Println("PowerShell AMSI event generated successfully")
		case "powershellspam":
			log.Println("Generating multiple PowerShell events...")
			cmd.WriteRandomPowerShellEvent()
			log.Println("PowerShell spam events generated successfully")
		}
	case "defender":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "defenderenabled":
			cmd.WriteDefenderEnabledEvent()
		case "defenderdisabled":
			cmd.WriteDefenderDisabledEvent()
		case "defendermalware":
			cmd.WriteDefenderMalwareDetectedEvent()
		case "spamdefender":
			cmd.WriteSpamDefenderEvent()
		}
	case "dotnet":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "dotnet":
			cmd.WriteDotNetEvent()
		case "maliciousdotnet":
			cmd.WriteMaliciousDotNetEvent()
		case "spamdotnet":
			cmd.WriteSpamDotNetEvent()
		}
	case "codeintegrity":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "codeintegrity-revokeddriver":
			log.Println("Generating CodeIntegrity CiRevokedDriverNotLoaded event (3023)...")
			cmd.WriteCodeIntegrityRevokedDriverEvent()
			log.Println("CodeIntegrity revoked driver event generated successfully")
		case "codeintegrity-revokedimage":
			log.Println("Generating CodeIntegrity CiRevokedImageNotLoaded event (3036)...")
			cmd.WriteCodeIntegrityRevokedImageEvent()
			log.Println("CodeIntegrity revoked image event generated successfully")
		case "codeintegrity-policyfailure":
			log.Println("Generating CodeIntegrity DeviceGuard policy failure audit event (3076)...")
			cmd.WriteCodeIntegrityPolicyFailureEvent()
			log.Println("CodeIntegrity policy failure audit event generated successfully")
		case "codeintegrity-policyfailureblock":
			log.Println("Generating CodeIntegrity DeviceGuard policy failure event (3077)...")
			cmd.WriteCodeIntegrityPolicyFailureBlockEvent()
			log.Println("CodeIntegrity policy failure block event generated successfully")

		case "codeintegrity-spam":
			log.Println("Generating multiple random CodeIntegrity events...")
			cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomCodeIntegrityEvents()
			log.Println("CodeIntegrity spam events completed")
		}
	case "applocker":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "applocker-processaudit":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Process Audit event (8003)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerProcessAuditEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker process audit event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-processblock":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Process Block event (8004)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerProcessBlockEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker process block event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-scriptaudit":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Script Audit event (8006)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerScriptAuditEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker script audit event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-scriptblock":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Script Block event (8007)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerScriptBlockEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker script block event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-appxprocessaudit":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Appx Process Audit event (8021)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerAppxProcessAuditEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker Appx process audit event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-appxprocessblock":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Appx Process Block event (8022)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerAppxProcessBlockEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker Appx process block event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-appxscriptaudit":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Appx Script Audit event (8024)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerAppxScriptAuditEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker Appx script audit event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-appxscriptblock":
			log.Println("Generating AppLocker Appx Script Block event (8025)...")
			cmd.WriteAppLockerAppxScriptBlockEvent()
			log.Println("AppLocker Appx script block event generated successfully")
		case "applocker-spam":
			log.Println("Generating multiple random AppLocker events...")
			cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomAppLockerEvents()
			log.Println("AppLocker spam events completed")
		}
	case "ntlm":
		switch m.subProvider {
		case "ntlm-blocking":
			log.Println("Generating NTLM blocking event (8001)...")
			cmd.WriteNTLMBlockingEvent()
			log.Println("NTLM blocking event generated successfully")
		case "ntlm-spam":
			log.Println("Generating multiple random NTLM blocking events...")
			cmd.WriteInfiniteRandomNTLMEvents()
			log.Println("NTLM spam events completed")
		}
	case "cyberevents":
		cmd.WriteCyberEvent()
	case "etwtraces":
		cmd.WriteETWTraceSession()
	}

	// Add completion message
	m.addLog(fmt.Sprintf("âœ… Completed: %s", m.getActionDescription()))
}

// View function
func (m model) View() string {
	if m.width == 0 {
		return "Loading..."
	}

	// Header
	header := titleStyle.Render("ðŸ›¡ï¸  BamboozlEDR - ETW Event Generator")

	// Create two columns: menu and logs
	var leftPanel, rightPanel string

	switch m.state {
	case stateMainMenu:
		leftPanel = menuStyle.Render(m.mainList.View())
	case stateSubMenu:
		leftPanel = menuStyle.Render(m.subList.View())
	case stateRunning:
		leftPanel = menuStyle.Render("Running: " + m.getActionDescription() + "\n\nPress ESC to stop")
	case stateBufferOverflow:
		statusText := "Buffer Overflow Mode\nMaximum Throughput\n\n"
		statusText += "ðŸš€ All ETW Providers Active\n"
		statusText += "ðŸ“Š Real-time Statistics â†’\n\n"
		statusText += "Press ESC to stop all functions"
		leftPanel = menuStyle.Render(statusText)
	}

	// Right panel with logs or stats
	var logTitle string
	var logContent string

	if m.state == stateBufferOverflow {
		// Show statistics table in the right panel during Buffer Overflow
		logTitle = titleStyle.Render("ðŸ“Š Buffer Overflow Statistics")
		if m.stats != "" {
			logContent = wrapText(m.stats, m.viewport.Width-2) // -2 for padding
		} else {
			logContent = "Initializing statistics...\nWaiting for ETW events..."
		}
	} else {
		// Show regular logs for all other states
		logTitle = titleStyle.Render("ðŸ“‹ Event Logs")
		logContent = m.viewport.View()
	}

	rightPanel = lipgloss.JoinVertical(lipgloss.Left, logTitle, logStyle.Render(logContent))

	// Combine panels
	mainContent := lipgloss.JoinHorizontal(lipgloss.Top, leftPanel, rightPanel)

	// Footer
	var help string
	if m.state == stateBufferOverflow || m.state == stateRunning {
		help = helpStyle.Render("ESC: stop â€¢ q: quit â€¢ PgUp/PgDn: scroll logs")
	} else {
		help = helpStyle.Render("â†‘/â†“: navigate â€¢ enter: select â€¢ esc: back â€¢ q: quit â€¢ PgUp/PgDn: scroll logs")
	}

	// Combine all
	return lipgloss.JoinVertical(
		lipgloss.Left,
		header,
		"",
		mainContent,
		"",
		help,
	)
}

// Custom log writer to capture log output
type logWriter struct {
	program *tea.Program
}

func (w *logWriter) Write(p []byte) (n int, err error) {
	if w.program != nil {
		w.program.Send(logMsg(strings.TrimSpace(string(p))))
	}
	return len(p), nil
}

func main() {
	internal.Banner()

	// Check for existing NotMDE ETW session before starting TUI (only if running as admin)
	if cmd.IsRunningAsAdmin() {
		cmd.CheckExistingETWSession()
	}

	// Create TUI model
	m := initialModel()

	// Start the TUI program
	p := tea.NewProgram(m, tea.WithAltScreen())

	// Set up custom log writer to capture all log output
	logWriter := &logWriter{program: p}
	log.SetOutput(logWriter)
	log.SetFlags(0) // Remove timestamp since we add our own

	if _, err := p.Run(); err != nil {
		log.Fatal(err)
	}
}
